<!-- Keywords: spec-kit, speckit, documentation-workflow, spec-folder, template-enforcement, context-preservation, progressive-documentation, validation, spec-kit-memory, vector-search, hybrid-search, bm25, rrf-fusion, fsrs-decay, constitutional-tier, checkpoint, importance-tiers, cognitive-memory, co-activation, tiered-injection -->

# Spec Kit - Mandatory Conversation Documentation

Orchestrates mandatory spec folder creation for all conversations involving file modifications. Ensures proper documentation level selection (1-3+), template usage, and context preservation through AGENTS.md-enforced workflows.


<!-- ANCHOR:when-to-use -->
## 1. WHEN TO USE

### What is a Spec Folder?

A **spec folder** is a numbered directory (e.g., `007-auth-feature/`) that contains documentation for a single feature/task or a coordinated packet of related phase work:

Spec folders may also be nested as coordination-root packets with direct-child phase folders (e.g., `specs/02--track/022-feature/011-phase/002-child/`).

- **Purpose**: Track specifications, plans, tasks, and decisions for one unit of work
- **Location**: Under `specs/` using either `###-short-name/` at the root or nested packet paths for phased coordination
- **Contents**: Markdown files (spec.md, plan.md, tasks.md, and implementation-summary.md when work is complete) plus optional support folders such as `scratch/`, `research/`, or `review/`

Think of it as a "project folder" for AI-assisted development - it keeps context organized and enables session continuity.

### Activation Triggers

**MANDATORY for ALL file modifications:**
- Code files: JS, TS, Python, CSS, HTML
- Documentation: Markdown, README, guides
- Configuration: JSON, YAML, TOML, env templates
- Templates, knowledge base, build/tooling files

**Request patterns that trigger activation:**
- "Add/implement/create [feature]"
- "Fix/update/refactor [code]"
- "Modify/change [configuration]"
- Any keyword: add, implement, fix, update, create, modify, rename, delete, configure, analyze, phase

**Example triggers:**
- "Add email validation to the signup form" → Level 1-2
- "Refactor the authentication module" → Level 2-3
- "Fix the button alignment bug" → Level 1
- "Implement user dashboard with analytics" → Level 3

### When NOT to Use

- Pure exploration/reading (no file modifications)
- Single typo fixes (<5 characters in one file)
- Whitespace-only changes
- Auto-generated file updates (package-lock.json)
- User explicitly selects Option D (skip documentation)

**Rule of thumb:** If modifying ANY file content → Activate this skill.
Status: ✅ This requirement applies immediately once file edits are requested.

### Distributed Governance Rule

Any agent writing authored spec folder docs (`spec.md`, `plan.md`, `tasks.md`, `checklist.md`, `implementation-summary.md`, `decision-record.md`, `handover.md`, `review-report.md`, `debug-delegation.md`, `resource-map.md` (optional)) MUST use templates from .opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/templates/level_N/ for level-owned docs and the root cross-cutting templates where applicable, run `bash .opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/scripts/spec/validate.sh [spec_folder] --strict` after each file write, and route continuity updates through /memory:save. Deep-research workflow-owned packet markdown (`research/iterations/*.md`, `research/deep-research-*.md`, and progressive `research/research.md` loop updates) is exempt from that generic per-write rule; `/spec_kit:deep-research` must instead run targeted strict validation after every `spec.md` mutation it performs. @deep-research retains exclusive write access for `research/research.md`; @debug retains exclusive write access for `debug-delegation.md`.

- `handover.md` stays in the canonical recovery ladder and is maintained through `/memory:save` handover_state routing using `.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/templates/handover.md` for initial creation.
- `review-report.md` remains owned by `@deep-review` when deep review workflows synthesize findings.
- `resource-map.md` is a peer cross-cutting template under `.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/templates/`; it remains optional at any level and gives reviewers a lean file ledger alongside `implementation-summary.md`.

### Utility Template Triggers

| Template              | Trigger Keywords                                                                                                              | Action                    |
| --------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ------------------------- |
| `handover.md`         | "handover", "next session", "continue later", "pass context", "ending session", "save state", "multi-session", "for next AI"  | Suggest `/memory:save` handover maintenance |
| `debug-delegation.md` | "stuck", "can't fix", "tried everything", "same error", "fresh eyes", "hours on this", "still failing", "need help debugging" | Suggest Task-tool debug delegation |

**Rule:** When detected, proactively suggest the appropriate action.

---

<!-- /ANCHOR:when-to-use -->
<!-- ANCHOR:smart-routing -->
## 2. SMART ROUTING

### Resource Domains

The router discovers markdown resources recursively from `references/` and `assets/` and then applies intent scoring from `RESOURCE_MAP`. Keep this section domain-focused rather than static file inventories.

- `references/memory/` for context retrieval, save workflows, trigger behavior, and indexing.
- `references/templates/` for level selection, template composition, and structure guides.
- `references/validation/` for checklist policy, verification rules, decision formats, and template compliance contracts.
- `references/structure/` for folder organization and sub-folder versioning.
- `references/workflows/` for command workflows and worked examples.
- `references/debugging/` for troubleshooting and root-cause methodology.
- `references/config/` for runtime environment configuration.

### Template and Script Sources of Truth

- Level definitions and template size guidance: [level_specifications.md](./references/templates/level_specifications.md)
- Template usage and composition rules: [template_guide.md](./references/templates/template_guide.md)
- Use `templates/level_N/` for operational templates; `core/` and `addendum/` remain composition inputs.
- Use `templates/changelog/` for packet-local nested changelog generation at completion time.
- Script architecture, build outputs, and runtime entrypoints: [scripts/README.md](./scripts/README.md)
- Memory save JSON schema and workflow contracts: [save_workflow.md](./references/memory/save_workflow.md)
- Nested packet changelog workflow: [nested_changelog.md](./references/workflows/nested_changelog.md)

Primary operational scripts:
- `spec/validate.sh`
- `spec/create.sh`
- `spec/archive.sh`
- `spec/check-completion.sh`
- `spec/recommend-level.sh`
- `templates/compose.sh`

### Resource Loading Levels

| Level       | When to Load               | Resources                    |
| ----------- | -------------------------- | ---------------------------- |
| ALWAYS      | Every skill invocation     | Shared patterns + SKILL.md   |
| CONDITIONAL | If intent signals match   | Intent-mapped references     |
| ON_DEMAND   | Only on explicit request   | Deep-dive quality standards  |

`references/workflows/quick_reference.md` is the primary first-touch command surface. Keep the compact `spec_kit` and `memory` command map there, including `/spec_kit:plan --intake-only` as the standalone intake entry, `/spec_kit:plan` and `/spec_kit:complete` smart delegation notes, and the pointer from `/spec_kit:deep-research` to `../sk-deep-research/references/spec_check_protocol.md`, and use this file only to point readers to it rather than duplicating the full matrix.

### Smart Router Pseudocode

The authoritative routing logic for scoped loading, weighted intent scoring, and ambiguity handling.

.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/mcp_server/README.md:270:**Confidence truncation** cuts off results at 2x the median score gap so you never get a long tail of irrelevant items.

.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/mcp_server/README.md:356:**Auto-promotion** -- memories earn their way up. After 5 positive validation marks, a normal memory promotes to important. After 10, important promotes to critical. Rate-limited to prevent bulk promotion during busy sessions.
.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/mcp_server/README.md:372:The system tracks how decisions relate to each other. Think of it like a corkboard with sticky notes connected by string. One note says "we chose JWT tokens." A string connects it to "because the session store was too slow." Another string connects that to "the Redis outage on March 5th."
.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/mcp_server/README.md:448:**Session deduplication** -- pushes down results you already saw. If you got a result 3 turns ago, new searches rank it lower. Saves approximately 50% of tokens on follow-up queries.
.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/mcp_server/README.md:466:**Learned relevance feedback** -- watches when you mark results as useful or not. Helpful results get a boost in future queries. 10 safeguards prevent noise: denylist, rate limits, 30-day decay, per-cycle caps, minimum session thresholds, one-week trial period before boosts go live.
.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/mcp_server/README.md:494:**ANCHOR-based section retrieval** -- indexed packet docs and generated continuity artifacts can include `<!-- ANCHOR:name -->` markers. The search system indexes individual sections separately, allowing retrieval of just "decisions" or "next-steps" from a large document (~93% token savings). Files above 50K characters are always chunk-split.
.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/mcp_server/README.md:542:**Architecture:** CocoIndex (semantic, external MCP) finds code by concept. Code Graph (structural, this server) maps imports, calls and hierarchy. Memory (session, this server) preserves decisions. The compact-merger combines all three under a 4000-token budget for compaction injection. Code-graph source is self-contained under `code-graph/` with `handlers/`, `lib/`, `tools/`, and `tests/`.
.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/mcp_server/README.md:586:**Affordance evidence:** `advisor_recommend` accepts structured tool/resource hints as a sanitized affordance lane wired into the existing `derived_generated` and `graph_causal` lanes — no new scoring lane, no new `entity_kind`, no new relation type. The allowlist normalizer at `skill_advisor/lib/affordance-normalizer.ts` accepts only `skillId`/`skill_id`, `name`, `triggers[]`, `category`, and the existing relation fields (`dependsOn[]`/`depends_on[]`, `enhances[]`, `siblings[]`, `prerequisiteFor[]`/`prerequisite_for[]`, `conflictsWith[]`/`conflicts_with[]`). Free-form `description` text is intentionally ignored as a trigger source. URLs, email addresses, token-shaped fragments, control characters, and instruction-shaped strings are stripped or dropped before scoring. Sanitized triggers contribute through the existing `derived_generated` lane (`scorer/lanes/derived.ts`) with reduced weight, and normalized relations become temporary edges in the existing `graph_causal` lane (`scorer/lanes/graph-causal.ts`) reusing the existing `enhances` / `siblings` / `depends_on` / `prerequisite_for` / `conflicts_with` `EDGE_MULTIPLIER` values. Recommendation payloads cite stable `affordance:<skillId>:<index>` identifiers — never raw matched phrases. The Python graph compiler (`skill_advisor/scripts/skill_graph_compiler.py`) compiles `derived.affordances[]` into existing `signals` and sparse adjacency without changing `ALLOWED_ENTITY_KINDS` (`{"skill", "agent", "script", "config", "reference"}`).

.opencode/skill/system-spec-kit/mcp_server/README.md:1075:Get LLM-oriented compact graph neighborhoods. Accepts CocoIndex search results as seeds for structural expansion. Modes: `neighborhood` (1-hop calls plus imports), `outline` (file symbols), `impact` (reverse callers). Successful responses return `status: "ok"` plus readiness/trust metadata, resolved anchors, graph context, and `data.metadata.partialOutput` so callers can see whether deadline or token-budget pressure produced partial output. When the read path determines the graph needs a full scan, the tool returns an explicit `status: "blocked"` payload with `data.blocked`, `graphAnswersOmitted`, `requiredAction: "code_graph_scan"`, and the same readiness/trust metadata instead of partial graph answers.

Use it to distinguish a complete answer from one shortened by deadline or token-budget limits. `data.metadata.deadlineMs` exposes the effective per-call deadline so callers can correlate `partialOutput.reasons` with the budget that produced them.

   121	/* ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   122	   3. TOOL-TO-LAYER MAPPING
   123	
   124	   Maps each tool to its layer for quick lookup.
   125	   ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */
   126	
   127	/**
   128	 * Defines the TOOL_LAYER_MAP constant.
   129	 */
   130	export const TOOL_LAYER_MAP: Record<string, LayerId> = {} as Record<string, LayerId>;
   131	for (const [layerId, layer] of Object.entries(LAYER_DEFINITIONS)) {
   132	  for (const tool of layer.tools) {
   133	    (TOOL_LAYER_MAP as Record<string, string>)[tool] = layerId;
   134	  }
   135	}
   136	
   137	/* ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   138	   4. LAYER PREFIX GENERATOR
   139	
   140	   Generates description prefixes for tool descriptions.
   141	   Format: "[L#:Name] Original description..."
   142	   ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */
   143	
   144	/**
   145	 * Get the layer ID for a tool.
   146	 */
   147	export function getLayerForTool(toolName: string): LayerId | null {
   148	  return TOOL_LAYER_MAP[toolName] ?? null;
   149	}
   150	
   151	/**
   152	 * Get the layer prefix for a tool's description.
   153	 * CHK-073: Tool descriptions include layer prefix.
   154	 */
   155	export function getLayerPrefix(toolName: string): string {
   156	  const layerId = getLayerForTool(toolName);
   157	  if (!layerId) return '';
   158	
   159	  const layer = LAYER_DEFINITIONS[layerId];
   160	  return `[${layerId}:${layer.name}]`;
   161	}
   162	
   163	/**
   164	 * Enhance a tool description with layer information.
   165	 * CHK-073: Adds layer prefix to description.
   166	 */
   167	export function enhanceDescription(toolName: string, description: string): string {
   168	  const prefix = getLayerPrefix(toolName);
   169	  if (!prefix) return description;
   170	
   171	  return `${prefix} ${description}`;
   172	}
   173	
   174	/* ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   175	   5. TOKEN BUDGET HELPERS
   176	
   177	   CHK-072: Token budgets assigned per layer.
   178	   ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */
   179	
   180	/**
   181	 * Get the token budget for a tool.
   182	 */
   183	export function getLayerTokenBudget(toolName: string): number {
   184	  const layerId = getLayerForTool(toolName);
   185	  if (!layerId) return 1000; // Default budget
   186	
   187	  return LAYER_DEFINITIONS[layerId].tokenBudget;
   188	}
   189	
   190	/**
   191	 * Get the token budget for a tool.
   192	 */
   193	export function getTokenBudget(toolName: string): number {
   194	  return getLayerTokenBudget(toolName);
   195	}
   196	
   197	/**
   198	 * Get layer information for a tool.
   199	 */
   200	export function getLayerInfo(toolName: string): LayerDefinition | null {
   201	  const layerId = getLayerForTool(toolName);
   202	  if (!layerId) return null;
   203	
   204	  return { ...LAYER_DEFINITIONS[layerId] };
   205	}
   206	
   207	/**
   208	 * Get all layers in priority order.
   209	 */
   210	export function getLayersByPriority(): LayerDefinition[] {
   211	  return Object.values(LAYER_DEFINITIONS).sort((a, b) => a.priority - b.priority);
   212	}

  1339	
  1340	async function enrichFusedResults(
  1341	  query: string,
  1342	  execution: HybridFusionExecution,
  1343	  options: HybridSearchOptions = {},
  1344	  initialResults: HybridSearchResult[] = execution.fusedResults
  1345	): Promise<HybridSearchResult[]> {
  1346	  const {
  1347	    evaluationMode,
  1348	    intent,
  1349	    lists,
  1350	    routeResult,
  1351	    budgetResult,
  1352	    s3meta,
  1353	    vectorEmbeddingCache,
  1354	  } = execution;
  1355	  let fusedHybridResults = initialResults;
  1356	  const limit = options.limit || DEFAULT_LIMIT;
  1357	
  1358	  // -- Aggregation stage: MPAB chunk-to-memory aggregation (after fusion, before state filter) --
  1359	  // When enabled, collapses chunk-level results back to their parent memory
  1360	  // Documents using MPAB scoring (sMax + 0.3 * sum(remaining) / sqrt(N)). This prevents
  1361	  // Multiple chunks from the same document dominating the result list.
  1362	  // MINOR-1 fix: isMpabEnabled() and isDocscoreAggregationEnabled() check the same env var
  1363	  if (isDocscoreAggregationEnabled()) {
  1364	    try {
  1365	      const chunkResults = fusedHybridResults.filter(
  1366	        r => (r as Record<string, unknown>).parentMemoryId != null && (r as Record<string, unknown>).chunkIndex != null
  1367	      );
  1368	      if (chunkResults.length > 0) {
  1369	        const nonChunkResults = fusedHybridResults.filter(
  1370	          r => (r as Record<string, unknown>).parentMemoryId == null || (r as Record<string, unknown>).chunkIndex == null
  1371	        );
  1372	        const collapsed = collapseAndReassembleChunkResults(
  1373	          chunkResults.map(r => ({
  1374	            id: r.id,
  1375	            parentMemoryId: (r as Record<string, unknown>).parentMemoryId as number | string,
  1376	            chunkIndex: (r as Record<string, unknown>).chunkIndex as number,
  1377	            score: r.score,
  1378	          }))
  1379	        );
  1380	        // Merge collapsed chunk results with non-chunk results
  1381	        fusedHybridResults = [
  1382	          ...collapsed.map(c => ({
  1383	            id: c.parentMemoryId,
  1384	            score: c.mpabScore,
  1385	            source: 'mpab' as string,
  1386	            _chunkHits: c._chunkHits,
  1387	          } as HybridSearchResult)),
  1388	          ...nonChunkResults,
  1389	        ];
  1390	      }
  1391	    } catch (_mpabErr: unknown) {
  1392	      // Non-critical — MPAB failure does not block pipeline
  1393	      const msg = _mpabErr instanceof Error ? _mpabErr.message : String(_mpabErr);
  1394	      console.error('[hybrid-search] MPAB error (non-fatal):', msg);
  1395	    }
  1396	  }
  1397	
  1398	  // -- Stage C: Channel Enforcement (SPECKIT_CHANNEL_MIN_REP) --
  1399	  // Ensures every channel that returned results has at least one representative
  1400	  // In the top-k window. Prevents single-channel dominance in fusion output.
  1401	  // When disabled, passes results through unchanged.
  1402	  try {
  1403	    const channelResultSets = new Map<string, Array<{ id: number | string; score: number; [key: string]: unknown }>>();
  1404	    for (const list of lists) {
  1405	      channelResultSets.set(list.source, list.results.map(r => ({
  1406	        ...r,
  1407	        id: r.id,
  1408	        score: typeof (r as Record<string, unknown>).score === 'number'
  1409	          ? (r as Record<string, unknown>).score as number
  1410	          : typeof (r as Record<string, unknown>).similarity === 'number'
  1411	            ? ((r as Record<string, unknown>).similarity as number) / 100
  1412	            : 0,
  1413	      })));
  1414	    }
  1415	
  1416	    const enforcementResult: EnforcementResult = enforceChannelRepresentation(
  1417	      fusedHybridResults.map(r => ({ ...r, source: r.source || 'hybrid' })),
  1418	      channelResultSets,
  1419	      limit,
  1420	    );
  1421	
  1422	    if (enforcementResult.enforcement.applied) {
  1423	      fusedHybridResults = enforcementResult.results as HybridSearchResult[];
  1424	      s3meta.enforcement = {
  1425	        applied: true,
  1426	        promotedCount: enforcementResult.enforcement.promotedCount,
  1427	        underRepresentedChannels: enforcementResult.enforcement.underRepresentedChannels,
  1428	      };
  1429	    }
  1430	  } catch (err: unknown) {
  1431	    // Non-critical — enforcement failure does not block pipeline
  1432	    console.warn('[hybrid-search] channel enforcement failed:', err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err));
  1433	  }
  1434	
  1435	  // Preserve non-enumerable eval metadata across later array reallocations.
  1436	  const shadowMeta = initialResults as HybridSearchResult[] & ShadowMetaArray;
  1437	  const s4shadowMeta = shadowMeta._s4shadow;
  1438	  const s4attributionMeta = shadowMeta._s4attribution;
  1439	  const degradationMeta = shadowMeta._degradation;
  1440	
  1441	  // C138/T316: MMR reranking with request-scoped embedding cache.
  1442	  // Reuse embeddings already returned by the vector channel when present and
  1443	  // only query vec_memories for missing IDs.
  1444	  let reranked: HybridSearchResult[] = fusedHybridResults.slice(0, limit);
  1445	
  1446	  // P1-5: Optional local GGUF reranking path (RERANKER_LOCAL=true).
  1447	  // Preserve cross-encoder gate semantics: when SPECKIT_CROSS_ENCODER=false, skip reranking.
  1448	  if (isCrossEncoderEnabled() && isLocalRerankerEnabled() && reranked.length >= MMR_MIN_CANDIDATES) {
  1449	    const localReranked = await rerankLocal(query, reranked, limit);
  1450	    if (localReranked !== reranked) {
  1451	      reranked = localReranked as HybridSearchResult[];
  1452	    }
  1453	  }
  1454	
  1455	  if (db && isMMREnabled()) {
  1456	    const numericIds = reranked
  1457	      .map(r => r.id)
  1458	      .filter((id): id is number => typeof id === 'number');
  1459	
  1460	    if (numericIds.length >= MMR_MIN_CANDIDATES) {
  1461	      try {
  1462	        const embeddingMap = new Map<number, Float32Array>(vectorEmbeddingCache);
  1463	        const missingIds = numericIds.filter((id) => !embeddingMap.has(id));
  1464	
  1465	        if (missingIds.length > 0) {
  1466	          const placeholders = missingIds.map(() => '?').join(', ');
  1467	          const embRows = (db.prepare(
  1468	            `SELECT rowid, embedding FROM vec_memories WHERE rowid IN (${placeholders})`
  1469	          ) as Database.Statement).all(...missingIds) as Array<{ rowid: number; embedding: Buffer }>;
  1470	
  1471	          for (const row of embRows) {
  1472	            if (Buffer.isBuffer(row.embedding)) {
  1473	              embeddingMap.set(
  1474	                row.rowid,
  1475	                new Float32Array(row.embedding.buffer, row.embedding.byteOffset, row.embedding.byteLength / 4)
  1476	              );
  1477	            }
  1478	          }
  1479	        }
  1480	
  1481	        const mmrCandidates: MMRCandidate[] = [];
  1482	        for (const r of reranked) {
  1483	          const emb = embeddingMap.get(r.id as number);
  1484	          if (emb) {
  1485	            mmrCandidates.push({
  1486	              id: r.id as number,
  1487	              score: (r.score as number) ?? 0,
  1488	              embedding: emb,
  1489	            });
  1490	          }
  1491	        }
  1492	
  1493	        if (mmrCandidates.length >= MMR_MIN_CANDIDATES) {
  1494	          const mmrLambda = INTENT_LAMBDA_MAP[intent] ?? MMR_DEFAULT_LAMBDA;
  1495	          const diversified = applyMMR(mmrCandidates, { lambda: mmrLambda, limit });
  1496	
  1497	          // FIX #6: Same fix as stage3-rerank FIX #5 — MMR can only diversify
  1498	          // rows that have embeddings. Non-embedded rows (lexical-only hits,
  1499	          // graph injections) must be preserved and merged back in their
  1500	          // original relative order instead of being silently dropped.
  1501	          const embeddedIdSet = new Set(mmrCandidates.map(c => c.id));
  1502	          const nonEmbeddedRows = reranked.filter(r => !embeddedIdSet.has(r.id as number));
  1503	          const rerankedById = new Map<string, HybridSearchResult>(
  1504	            reranked.map((result) => [canonicalResultId(result.id), result])
  1505	          );
  1506	
  1507	          const diversifiedRows = diversified.map((candidate): HybridSearchResult => {
  1508	            const existing = rerankedById.get(canonicalResultId(candidate.id));
  1509	            if (existing) {
  1510	              return existing;
  1511	            }
  1512	
  1513	            return {
  1514	              id: candidate.id,
  1515	              score: candidate.score,
  1516	              source: 'vector',
  1517	            };
  1518	          });
  1519	
  1520	          // Merge: diversified embedded rows first (MMR-ordered), then
  1521	          // non-embedded rows in their original relative order.
  1522	          reranked = [...diversifiedRows, ...nonEmbeddedRows];
  1523	        }
  1524	      } catch (embErr: unknown) {
  1525	        const msg = embErr instanceof Error ? embErr.message : String(embErr);
  1526	        console.warn(`[hybrid-search] MMR embedding retrieval failed: ${msg}`);
  1527	      }
  1528	    }
  1529	  }
  1530	
  1531	  // C138: Co-activation spreading — enrich with temporal neighbors
  1532	  const topIds = reranked
  1533	    .slice(0, SPREAD_ACTIVATION_TOP_N)
  1534	    .map(r => r.id)
  1535	    .filter((id): id is number => typeof id === 'number');
  1536	  if (topIds.length > 0) {
  1537	    try {
  1538	      const spreadResults: SpreadResult[] = spreadActivation(topIds);
  1539	      // Boost scores of results that appear in co-activation graph
  1540	      if (spreadResults.length > 0) {
  1541	        const spreadMap = new Map(spreadResults.map(sr => [sr.id, sr.activationScore]));
  1542	        for (const result of reranked) {
  1543	          const boost = spreadMap.get(result.id as number);
  1544	          if (boost !== undefined) {
  1545	            // M10 FIX: Update all score aliases so downstream consumers see the boost
  1546	            const boostedScore = ((result.score as number) ?? 0) + boost * CO_ACTIVATION_CONFIG.boostFactor;
  1547	            (result as Record<string, unknown>).score = boostedScore;
  1548	            if ('rrfScore' in result) (result as Record<string, unknown>).rrfScore = boostedScore;
  1549	            if ('intentAdjustedScore' in result) (result as Record<string, unknown>).intentAdjustedScore = boostedScore;
  1550	          }
  1551	        }
  1552	      }
  1553	      // P1-2 FIX: Re-sort after co-activation boost to ensure boosted results
  1554	      // Are promoted to their correct position in the ranking
  1555	      reranked.sort((a, b) => ((b.score as number) ?? 0) - ((a.score as number) ?? 0));
  1556	    } catch (err: unknown) {
  1557	      // Non-critical enrichment — co-activation failure does not affect core ranking
  1558	      console.warn('[hybrid-search] co-activation enrichment failed:', err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err));
  1559	    }
  1560	  }
  1561	
  1562	  // Folder relevance / two-pass retrieval (SPECKIT_FOLDER_SCORING)
  1563	  if (db && isFolderScoringEnabled() && reranked.length > 0) {
  1564	    try {
  1565	      const numericIds = reranked
  1566	        .map(r => r.id)
  1567	        .filter((id): id is number => typeof id === 'number');
  1568	
  1569	      if (numericIds.length > 0) {
  1570	        const folderMap = lookupFolders(db, numericIds);
  1571	        if (folderMap.size > 0) {
  1572	          const folderScores = computeFolderRelevanceScores(reranked, folderMap);
  1573	          const rawTopK = process.env.SPECKIT_FOLDER_TOP_K;
  1574	          const parsedTopK = rawTopK ? parseInt(rawTopK, 10) : NaN;
  1575	          const topK = Number.isFinite(parsedTopK) && parsedTopK > 0 ? parsedTopK : 5;
  1576	
  1577	          const twoPhaseResults = twoPhaseRetrieval(reranked, folderScores, folderMap, topK);
  1578	          const postFolderResults = twoPhaseResults.length > 0 ? twoPhaseResults : reranked;
  1579	          reranked = enrichResultsWithFolderScores(postFolderResults, folderScores, folderMap) as HybridSearchResult[];
  1580	        }
  1581	      }
  1582	    } catch (_folderErr: unknown) {
  1583	      // Folder scoring is optional and must not break retrieval
  1584	    }
  1585	  }
  1586	
  1587	  // -- Stage D: Confidence Truncation (SPECKIT_CONFIDENCE_TRUNCATION) --
  1588	  // Run after the ranking pipeline so later boosts/promotions can rescue
  1589	  // candidates before low-confidence tails are trimmed.
  1590	  if (!evaluationMode) {
  1591	    try {
  1592	      const truncationResult: TruncationResult = truncateByConfidence(
  1593	        reranked.map(r => ({ ...r, id: r.id, score: r.score })),
  1594	      );
  1595	
  1596	      if (truncationResult.truncated) {
  1597	        reranked = truncationResult.results.map(r => r as HybridSearchResult);
  1598	        s3meta.truncation = {
  1599	          truncated: true,
  1600	          originalCount: truncationResult.originalCount,
  1601	          truncatedCount: truncationResult.truncatedCount,
  1602	          medianGap: truncationResult.medianGap,
  1603	          cutoffGap: truncationResult.cutoffGap,
  1604	          cutoffIndex: truncationResult.cutoffIndex,
  1605	          thresholdMultiplier: GAP_THRESHOLD_MULTIPLIER,
  1606	          minResultsGuaranteed: DEFAULT_MIN_RESULTS,
  1607	          featureFlagEnabled: isConfidenceTruncationEnabled(),
  1608	        };
  1609	      }
  1610	    } catch (err: unknown) {
  1611	      // Non-critical — truncation failure does not block pipeline
  1612	      console.warn('[hybrid-search] confidence truncation failed:', err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err));
  1613	    }
  1614	  }
  1615	
  1616	  // Preserve routing and Stage 4 trace metadata as explicit result fields so downstream
  1617	  // Formatters can opt-in to provenance-rich envelopes without relying on
  1618	  // Non-enumerable array shadow properties.
  1619	  if (reranked.length > 0) {
  1620	    reranked = reranked.map((row): HybridSearchResult => {
  1621	      const existingTraceMetadata =
  1622	        typeof row.traceMetadata === 'object' && row.traceMetadata !== null && !Array.isArray(row.traceMetadata)
  1623	          ? row.traceMetadata
  1624	          : {};
  1625	
  1626	      return {
  1627	        ...row,
  1628	        traceMetadata: {
  1629	          ...existingTraceMetadata,
  1630	          ...(s4shadowMeta !== undefined ? { stage4: s4shadowMeta } : {}),
  1631	          ...(s4attributionMeta !== undefined ? { attribution: s4attributionMeta } : {}),
  1632	          ...(degradationMeta !== undefined ? { degradation: degradationMeta } : {}),
  1633	          evaluationMode,
  1634	          // Wire queryComplexity from router classification into trace
  1635	          queryComplexity: routeResult.tier,
  1636	          // Wire confidence truncation metadata into per-result trace (036)
  1637	          ...(s3meta.truncation ? {
  1638	            confidenceTruncation: {
  1639	              truncated: s3meta.truncation.truncated,
  1640	              originalCount: s3meta.truncation.originalCount,
  1641	              truncatedCount: s3meta.truncation.truncatedCount,
  1642	              medianGap: s3meta.truncation.medianGap,
  1643	              cutoffGap: s3meta.truncation.cutoffGap,
  1644	              cutoffIndex: s3meta.truncation.cutoffIndex,
  1645	              thresholdMultiplier: s3meta.truncation.thresholdMultiplier,
  1646	              minResultsGuaranteed: s3meta.truncation.minResultsGuaranteed,
  1647	            },
  1648	          } : {}),
  1649	        },
  1650	      };
  1651	    });
  1652	  }
  1653	
  1654	  if (isContextHeadersEnabled() && reranked.length > 0) {
  1655	    const descriptionCache = buildDescriptionTailMap();
  1656	    if (descriptionCache.size > 0) {
  1657	      reranked = reranked.map((row) => injectContextualTree(row, descriptionCache));
  1658	    }
  1659	  }
  1660	
  1661	  let budgetTruncated = false;
  1662	  let budgetLimit: number | undefined;
  1663	  if (evaluationMode) {
  1664	    reranked = applyResultLimit(reranked, options.limit);
  1665	  } else {
  1666	    // Apply token budget truncation after trace/header enrichment so token
  1667	    // estimates reflect the actual returned payload shape.
  1668	    const headerOverhead = isContextHeadersEnabled()
  1669	      ? reranked.length * CONTEXT_HEADER_TOKEN_OVERHEAD
  1670	      : 0;
  1671	    const adjustedBudget = Math.max(budgetResult.budget - headerOverhead, 200);
  1672	
  1673	    if (s3meta.tokenBudget) {
  1674	      s3meta.tokenBudget.headerOverhead = headerOverhead;
  1675	      s3meta.tokenBudget.adjustedBudget = adjustedBudget;
  1676	    }
  1677	
  1678	    const budgeted = truncateToBudget(reranked, adjustedBudget, {
  1679	      includeContent: options.includeContent ?? false,
  1680	      queryId: `hybrid-${Date.now()}`,
  1681	    });
  1682	    reranked = budgeted.results;
  1683	    budgetTruncated = budgeted.truncated;
  1684	    budgetLimit = budgetResult.budget;
  1685	  }
  1686	
  1687	  if (reranked.length > 0) {
  1688	    reranked = reranked.map((row): HybridSearchResult => {
  1689	      const existingTraceMetadata =
  1690	        typeof row.traceMetadata === 'object' && row.traceMetadata !== null && !Array.isArray(row.traceMetadata)
  1691	          ? row.traceMetadata
  1692	          : {};
  1693	
  1694	      return {
  1695	        ...row,
  1696	        traceMetadata: {
  1697	          ...existingTraceMetadata,
  1698	          budgetTruncated,
  1699	          ...(budgetLimit !== undefined ? { budgetLimit } : {}),
  1700	        },
  1701	      };
  1702	    });
  1703	  }
  1704	
  1705	  if (s4shadowMeta !== undefined && reranked.length > 0) {
  1706	    Object.defineProperty(reranked, '_s4shadow', {
  1707	      value: s4shadowMeta,
  1708	      enumerable: false,

exec

 succeeded in 0ms:
  2250	  });
  2251	
  2252	  return finalResults;
  2253	}

  2255	// 14. PRE-FLIGHT TOKEN BUDGET VALIDATION (T007)
  2256	
  2257	/** Default token budget — configurable via SPECKIT_TOKEN_BUDGET env var. */
  2258	const DEFAULT_TOKEN_BUDGET = 2000;
  2259	
  2260	/** Maximum characters for a summary fallback when a single result overflows the budget. */
  2261	const SUMMARY_MAX_CHARS = 400;
  2262	
  2263	/** Overflow log entry recording budget truncation events for eval infrastructure. */
  2264	interface OverflowLogEntry {
  2265	  queryId: string;
  2266	  candidateCount: number;
  2267	  totalTokens: number;
  2268	  budgetLimit: number;
  2269	  truncatedToCount: number;
  2270	  timestamp: string;
  2271	}
  2272	
  2273	/** Result of budget-aware truncation. */
  2274	interface TruncateToBudgetResult {
  2275	  results: HybridSearchResult[];
  2276	  truncated: boolean;
  2277	  overflow?: OverflowLogEntry;
  2278	}
  2279	
  2280	/**
  2281	 * Estimate token count for a text string using a chars/4 heuristic.
  2282	 * @param text - The text to estimate tokens for.
  2283	 * @returns Approximate token count (ceiling of length / 4).
  2284	 */
  2285	function estimateTokenCount(text: string): number {
  2286	  if (!text) return 0;
  2287	  return Math.ceil(text.length / 4);
  2288	}
  2289	
  2290	function estimateStructuredValueChars(value: unknown, seen: WeakSet<object>): number {
  2291	  if (value == null) return 4;
  2292	
  2293	  if (typeof value === 'string') return value.length + 2;
  2294	  if (typeof value === 'number' || typeof value === 'bigint') return String(value).length;
  2295	  if (typeof value === 'boolean') return value ? 4 : 5;
  2296	
  2297	  if (Array.isArray(value)) {
  2298	    let chars = 2;
  2299	    for (const item of value) {
  2300	      chars += estimateStructuredValueChars(item, seen) + 1;
  2301	    }
  2302	    return chars;
  2303	  }
  2304	
  2305	  if (typeof value !== 'object') return 0;
  2306	  if (seen.has(value)) return 8;
  2307	  seen.add(value);
  2308	
  2309	  let chars = 2;
  2310	  for (const [key, nestedValue] of Object.entries(value as Record<string, unknown>)) {
  2311	    chars += key.length + 3;
  2312	    chars += estimateStructuredValueChars(nestedValue, seen) + 1;
  2313	  }
  2314	  return chars;
  2315	}
  2316	
  2317	/**
  2318	 * Estimate the token footprint of a single HybridSearchResult.
  2319	 * @param result - The search result to measure.
  2320	 * @returns Approximate token count based on serialized key-value lengths.
  2321	 */
  2322	function estimateResultTokens(result: HybridSearchResult): number {
  2323	  const record = result as Record<string, unknown>;
  2324	  const seen = new WeakSet<object>();
  2325	  const handledKeys = new Set([
  2326	    'id',
  2327	    'score',
  2328	    'source',
  2329	    'title',
  2330	    'content',
  2331	    'sources',
  2332	    'spec_folder',
  2333	    'file_path',
  2334	    'traceMetadata',
  2335	    'parentMemoryId',
  2336	    'chunkIndex',
  2337	    'similarity',
  2338	    'combined_lexical_score',
  2339	  ]);
  2340	
  2341	  let chars = 0;
  2342	  for (const key of handledKeys) {
  2343	    if (!(key in record)) continue;
  2344	    chars += key.length + 3;
  2345	    chars += estimateStructuredValueChars(record[key], seen) + 1;
  2346	  }
  2347	
  2348	  for (const key of Object.keys(record)) {
  2349	    if (handledKeys.has(key)) continue;
  2350	    const value = record[key];
  2351	    chars += key.length + 3;
  2352	    chars += estimateStructuredValueChars(value, seen) + 1;
  2353	  }
  2354	
  2355	  return Math.ceil(chars / 4);
  2356	}
  2357	
  2358	/**
  2359	 * Read the configured token budget from SPECKIT_TOKEN_BUDGET env var,
  2360	 * falling back to DEFAULT_TOKEN_BUDGET (2000).
  2361	 * @returns The effective token budget for result truncation.
  2362	 */
  2363	function getTokenBudget(): number {
  2364	  const envVal = process.env['SPECKIT_TOKEN_BUDGET'];
  2365	  if (envVal) {
  2366	    const parsed = parseInt(envVal, 10);
  2367	    if (!isNaN(parsed) && parsed > 0) return parsed;
  2368	  }
  2369	  return DEFAULT_TOKEN_BUDGET;
  2370	}
  2371	
  2372	/**
  2373	 * Create a summary fallback for a single result whose content exceeds the token budget.
  2374	 */
  2375	function createSummaryFallback(result: HybridSearchResult, budget: number): HybridSearchResult {
  2376	  const content = typeof result['content'] === 'string' ? result['content'] as string : '';
  2377	  const title = typeof result['title'] === 'string' ? result['title'] : 'Untitled';
  2378	
  2379	  const maxSummaryChars = Math.min(SUMMARY_MAX_CHARS, budget * 4);
  2380	  const truncatedContent = content.length > maxSummaryChars
  2381	    ? content.slice(0, maxSummaryChars) + '...'
  2382	    : content;
  2383	
  2384	  return {
  2385	    ...result,
  2386	    content: `[Summary] ${title}: ${truncatedContent}`,
  2387	    _summarized: true,
  2388	  };
  2389	}
  2390	
  2391	/**
  2392	 * Truncate a result set to fit within a token budget using greedy highest-scoring-first strategy.
  2393	 * @param results - The full result set to truncate.
  2394	 * @param budget - Optional token budget override (defaults to SPECKIT_TOKEN_BUDGET env / 2000).
  2395	 * @param options - Optional includeContent flag and queryId for overflow logging.
  2396	 * @returns Object with truncated results, truncation flag, and optional overflow log entry.
  2397	 */
  2398	function truncateToBudget(
  2399	  results: HybridSearchResult[],
  2400	  budget?: number,
  2401	  options?: { includeContent?: boolean; queryId?: string }
  2402	): TruncateToBudgetResult {
  2403	  const effectiveBudget = (budget && budget > 0) ? budget : getTokenBudget();
  2404	  const includeContent = options?.includeContent ?? false;
  2405	  const queryId = options?.queryId ?? `q-${Date.now()}`;
  2406	
  2407	  if (results.length === 0) {
  2408	    return { results: [], truncated: false };
  2409	  }
  2410	
  2411	  const sorted = [...results].sort((a, b) => b.score - a.score);
  2412	  const tokenEstimateCache = new Map<string, number>();
  2413	  const getTokenEstimate = (result: HybridSearchResult): number => {
  2414	    const cacheKey = canonicalResultId(result.id);
  2415	    const cached = tokenEstimateCache.get(cacheKey);
  2416	    if (cached !== undefined) {
  2417	      return cached;
  2418	    }
  2419	
  2420	    const estimate = estimateResultTokens(result);
  2421	    tokenEstimateCache.set(cacheKey, estimate);
  2422	    return estimate;
  2423	  };
  2424	
  2425	  const totalTokens = sorted.reduce((sum, result) => sum + getTokenEstimate(result), 0);
  2426	
  2427	  if (totalTokens <= effectiveBudget) {
  2428	    return { results: sorted, truncated: false };
  2429	  }
  2430	
  2431	  // Single-result overflow: summarize when content is included, otherwise keep
  2432	  // the lone result and mark the overflow for callers.
  2433	  if (sorted.length === 1) {
  2434	    const outputResult = includeContent
  2435	      ? createSummaryFallback(sorted[0]!, effectiveBudget)
  2436	      : sorted[0]!;
  2437	    const overflow: OverflowLogEntry = {
  2438	      queryId,
  2439	      candidateCount: 1,
  2440	      totalTokens,
  2441	      budgetLimit: effectiveBudget,
  2442	      truncatedToCount: 1,
  2443	      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
  2444	    };
  2445	    console.warn(
  2446	      `[hybrid-search] Token budget overflow (single-result fallback): ` +
  2447	      `${totalTokens} tokens > ${effectiveBudget} budget`
  2448	    );
  2449	    return { results: [outputResult], truncated: true, overflow };
  2450	  }
  2451	
  2452	  // Greedy accumulation: take highest-scoring results until budget exhausted
  2453	  const accepted: HybridSearchResult[] = [];
  2454	  let accumulated = 0;
  2455	
  2456	  for (const result of sorted) {
  2457	    const tokens = getTokenEstimate(result);
  2458	    if (accumulated + tokens > effectiveBudget) {
  2459	      if (accepted.length > 0) {
  2460	        break;
  2461	      }
  2462	      continue;
  2463	    }
  2464	    accepted.push(result);
  2465	    accumulated += tokens;
  2466	    if (accumulated >= effectiveBudget) break;
  2467	  }
  2468	
  2469	  if (accepted.length === 0 && sorted.length > 0) {
  2470	    const outputResult = includeContent
  2471	      ? createSummaryFallback(sorted[0]!, effectiveBudget)
  2472	      : sorted[0]!;
  2473	    const overflow: OverflowLogEntry = {
  2474	      queryId,
  2475	      candidateCount: results.length,
  2476	      totalTokens,
  2477	      budgetLimit: effectiveBudget,
  2478	      truncatedToCount: 1,
  2479	      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
  2480	    };
  2481	
  2482	    console.warn(
  2483	      `[hybrid-search] Token budget overflow (top-result fallback): ` +
  2484	      `${totalTokens} tokens > ${effectiveBudget} budget`
  2485	    );
  2486	
  2487	    return { results: [outputResult], truncated: true, overflow };
  2488	  }
  2489	
  2490	  const overflow: OverflowLogEntry = {
  2491	    queryId,
  2492	    candidateCount: results.length,
  2493	    totalTokens,
  2494	    budgetLimit: effectiveBudget,
  2495	    truncatedToCount: accepted.length,
  2496	    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
  2497	  };
  2498	
  2499	  console.warn(
  2500	    `[hybrid-search] Token budget overflow: ${totalTokens} tokens > ${effectiveBudget} budget, ` +
  2501	    `truncated ${results.length} → ${accepted.length} results`
  2502	  );
  2503	
  2504	  return { results: accepted, truncated: true, overflow };
  2505	}

 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
     2	// MODULE: Confidence Truncation
     3	// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
     4	// Feature catalog: Confidence-based result truncation
     5	import { isConfidenceTruncationEnabled } from './search-flags.js';
     6	
     7	/* --- 1. TYPES & CONSTANTS --- */
     8	
     9	/** Generic scored result for truncation — supports both numeric and string IDs. */
    10	interface ScoredResult {
    11	  id: number | string;
    12	  score: number;
    13	  [key: string]: unknown;
    14	}
    15	
    16	/** Result of a truncation operation with full audit metadata. */
    17	interface TruncationResult {
    18	  results: ScoredResult[];
    19	  truncated: boolean;
    20	  originalCount: number;
    21	  truncatedCount: number;
    22	  /** Inclusive index of the last kept result (0-based). */
    23	  cutoffIndex: number;
    24	  medianGap: number;
    25	  cutoffGap: number;
    26	}
    27	
    28	/** Options for truncation behaviour. */
    29	interface TruncationOptions {
    30	  /** Minimum number of results to always return, regardless of gap. Default: 3. */
    31	  minResults?: number;
    32	}
    33	
    34	/** Default minimum result count. */
    35	const DEFAULT_MIN_RESULTS = 3;
    36	
    37	/** Gap multiplier: gap must exceed this multiple of the median gap to trigger truncation.
    38	 * 2x median is the elbow heuristic — a gap twice the typical spread signals a relevance cliff. */
    39	const GAP_THRESHOLD_MULTIPLIER = 2;
    40	
    41	/* --- 2. GAP ANALYSIS HELPERS --- */
    42	
    43	/**
    44	 * Compute consecutive score gaps for a sorted (descending) score array.
    45	 * gap[i] = scores[i] - scores[i+1]   for i in [0, n-2]
    46	 * NaN and Infinity scores are filtered out before gap computation.
    47	 * Returns empty array when fewer than 2 finite scores.
    48	 *
    49	 * @param scores - Descending-sorted array of raw scores.
    50	 * @returns Array of consecutive score gaps (length = scores.length - 1).
    51	 */
    52	function computeGaps(scores: number[]): number[] {
    53	  // NaN/Infinity from upstream bugs would corrupt gap statistics — filter them first
    54	  const finite = scores.filter(s => Number.isFinite(s));
    55	  if (finite.length < 2) return [];
    56	  const gaps: number[] = [];
    57	  for (let i = 0; i < finite.length - 1; i++) {
    58	    gaps.push(finite[i] - finite[i + 1]);
    59	  }
    60	  return gaps;
    61	}
    62	
    63	/**
    64	 * Compute the median of an array of numbers.
    65	 * Returns 0 for an empty array.
    66	 *
    67	 * @param values - Array of numeric values.
    68	 * @returns Median value, or 0 for empty input.
    69	 */
    70	function computeMedian(values: number[]): number {
    71	  if (values.length === 0) return 0;
    72	  const sorted = [...values].sort((a, b) => a - b);
    73	  const mid = Math.floor(sorted.length / 2);
    74	  if (sorted.length % 2 === 1) {
    75	    return sorted[mid];
    76	  }
    77	  return (sorted[mid - 1] + sorted[mid]) / 2;
    78	}
    79	
    80	/* --- 3. CORE TRUNCATION LOGIC --- */
    81	
    82	/**
    83	 * Truncate results based on confidence gap analysis.
    84	 *
    85	 * Algorithm:
    86	 * 1. If fewer than minResults results, return unchanged.
    87	 * 2. Compute consecutive score gaps.
    88	 * 3. Compute median gap.
    89	 * 4. Find first index >= (minResults - 1) where gap > 2 * medianGap.
    90	 * 5. Truncate at that index + 1 (keep results 0..cutoffIndex inclusive).
    91	 * 6. If no threshold-exceeding gap found, return all results unchanged.
    92	 *
    93	 * When SPECKIT_CONFIDENCE_TRUNCATION is disabled, passes results through unchanged.
    94	 *
    95	 * Results are expected to be pre-sorted by score descending. This function
    96	 * does NOT sort; it operates on the input order.
    97	 *
    98	 * @param results - Array of scored results (expected descending by score).
    99	 * @param options - Optional truncation options (minResults).
   100	 * @returns TruncationResult with the (possibly shortened) result array and audit metadata.
   101	 */
   102	function truncateByConfidence(
   103	  results: ScoredResult[],
   104	  options?: TruncationOptions,
   105	): TruncationResult {
   106	  const minResults = options?.minResults ?? DEFAULT_MIN_RESULTS;
   107	
   108	  // Defensive: filter out results with NaN/Infinity scores
   109	  const validResults = results.filter(r => Number.isFinite(r.score));
   110	
   111	  // Defensive: sort descending by score. Callers should pre-sort for efficiency.
   112	  validResults.sort((a, b) => b.score - a.score);
   113	
   114	  const originalCount = validResults.length;
   115	
   116	  // Feature flag gate: pass through when disabled
   117	  if (!isConfidenceTruncationEnabled()) {
   118	    return {
   119	      results: [...validResults],
   120	      truncated: false,
   121	      originalCount,
   122	      truncatedCount: originalCount,
   123	      cutoffIndex: originalCount - 1,
   124	      medianGap: 0,
   125	      cutoffGap: 0,
   126	    };
   127	  }
   128	
   129	  // Not enough results to truncate
   130	  if (validResults.length <= minResults) {
   131	    return {
   132	      results: [...validResults],
   133	      truncated: false,
   134	      originalCount,
   135	      truncatedCount: originalCount,
   136	      cutoffIndex: originalCount - 1,
   137	      medianGap: 0,
   138	      cutoffGap: 0,
   139	    };
   140	  }
   141	
   142	  const scores = validResults.map(r => r.score);
   143	  const gaps = computeGaps(scores);
   144	  const medianGap = computeMedian(gaps);
   145	  const threshold = GAP_THRESHOLD_MULTIPLIER * medianGap;
   146	
   147	  // When medianGap is 0 (all same scores), no meaningful gap exists — return all
   148	  if (medianGap === 0) {
   149	    return {
   150	      results: [...validResults],
   151	      truncated: false,
   152	      originalCount,
   153	      truncatedCount: originalCount,
   154	      cutoffIndex: originalCount - 1,
   155	      medianGap: 0,
   156	      cutoffGap: 0,
   157	    };
   158	  }
   159	
   160	  // Search for the first gap that exceeds the threshold, starting from minResults - 1.
   161	  // Gap[i] is the gap between result i and result i+1.
   162	  // If gap[i] > threshold, we keep results 0..i (cutoffIndex = i).
   163	  let cutoffIndex = -1;
   164	  let cutoffGap = 0;
   165	
   166	  for (let i = minResults - 1; i < gaps.length; i++) {
   167	    if (gaps[i] > threshold) {
   168	      cutoffIndex = i;
   169	      cutoffGap = gaps[i];
   170	      break;
   171	    }
   172	  }
   173	
   174	  // No significant gap found — return all results
   175	  if (cutoffIndex === -1) {
   176	    return {
   177	      results: [...validResults],
   178	      truncated: false,
   179	      originalCount,
   180	      truncatedCount: originalCount,
   181	      cutoffIndex: originalCount - 1,
   182	      medianGap,
   183	      cutoffGap: 0,
   184	    };
   185	  }
   186	
   187	  // Truncate: keep validResults[0..cutoffIndex] inclusive
   188	  const truncatedResults = validResults.slice(0, cutoffIndex + 1);
   189	
   190	  return {
   191	    results: truncatedResults,
   192	    truncated: true,
   193	    originalCount,
   194	    truncatedCount: truncatedResults.length,
   195	    cutoffIndex,
   196	    medianGap,
   197	    cutoffGap,
   198	  };
   199	}
   200	
   201	/* --- 5. EXPORTS --- */
   202

   204	  // Types

   206	  type TruncationResult,
   207	  type TruncationOptions,
   208	
   209	  // Constants
   210	  DEFAULT_MIN_RESULTS,
   211	  GAP_THRESHOLD_MULTIPLIER,
   212	
   213	  // Functions
   214	  truncateByConfidence,
   215	  isConfidenceTruncationEnabled,
   216	
   217	  // Internal helpers (exported for testing)
   218	  computeGaps,
   219	  computeMedian,
   220	};

     2	// MODULE: Dynamic Token Budget
     3	// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
     4	//
     5	// ADVISORY-ONLY: This module computes a token budget for a query
     6	// Based on its complexity tier, but does NOT enforce that budget
     7	// Downstream. The returned BudgetResult is handed to callers who
     8	// Are solely responsible for respecting it (e.g. by trimming
     9	// Result sets or truncating content before sending to the LLM).
    10	import { type QueryComplexityTier } from './query-classifier.js';
    11	import { isDynamicTokenBudgetEnabled } from './search-flags.js';
    12	
    13	// Feature catalog: Dynamic token budget allocation
    14	
    15	
    16	/* --- 1. TYPES & CONSTANTS --- */
    17	
    18	/** Budget (in tokens) allocated per complexity tier. */
    19	interface TokenBudgetConfig {
    20	  /** Simple query budget: 1500 tokens. */
    21	  simple: number;
    22	  /** Moderate query budget: 2500 tokens. */
    23	  moderate: number;
    24	  /** Complex query budget: 4000 tokens. */
    25	  complex: number;
    26	}
    27	
    28	/** Result of a token budget lookup. */
    29	interface BudgetResult {
    30	  /** The complexity tier that determined the budget. */
    31	  tier: QueryComplexityTier;
    32	  /** The allocated token budget. */
    33	  budget: number;
    34	  /** Whether the dynamic flag was active (false = default fallback used). */
    35	  applied: boolean;
    36	}
    37	
    38	/** Default budget when the feature flag is disabled — treat everything as complex. */
    39	const DEFAULT_BUDGET = 4000;
    40	
    41	/** Default tier-to-budget mapping when dynamic allocation is enabled.
    42	 * 1500/2500/4000 tiers balance context window cost vs. recall —
    43	 * simple queries need fewer tokens, complex queries need the full budget. */
    44	const DEFAULT_TOKEN_BUDGET_CONFIG: TokenBudgetConfig = {
    45	  simple: 1500,
    46	  moderate: 2500,
    47	  complex: 4000,
    48	};
    49	
    50	/* --- 2. FEATURE FLAG --- */
    51	
    52	/* --- 3. BUDGET RESOLUTION --- */
    53	
    54	/**
    55	 * Get the token budget for a given query complexity tier.
    56	 *
    57	 * When SPECKIT_DYNAMIC_TOKEN_BUDGET is disabled (default), returns the DEFAULT_BUDGET
    58	 * (4000) for all queries regardless of tier, with applied=false.
    59	 *
    60	 * When enabled, maps tier to the configured budget:
    61	 *   simple   → 1500 tokens
    62	 *   moderate → 2500 tokens
    63	 *   complex  → 4000 tokens
    64	 *
    65	 * @param tier   - The complexity tier from the query classifier
    66	 * @param config - Optional custom budget config (overrides DEFAULT_TOKEN_BUDGET_CONFIG)
    67	 * @returns BudgetResult with tier, budget, and applied flag
    68	 */
    69	function getDynamicTokenBudget(
    70	  tier: QueryComplexityTier,
    71	  config?: TokenBudgetConfig,
    72	): BudgetResult {
    73	  // Feature flag gate: return default when disabled
    74	  if (!isDynamicTokenBudgetEnabled()) {
    75	    return {
    76	      tier,
    77	      budget: DEFAULT_BUDGET,
    78	      applied: false,
    79	    };
    80	  }
    81	
    82	  const effectiveConfig = config ?? DEFAULT_TOKEN_BUDGET_CONFIG;
    83	  const budget = effectiveConfig[tier] ?? DEFAULT_BUDGET;
    84	
    85	  return {
    86	    tier,
    87	    budget,
    88	    applied: true,
    89	  };
    90	}
    91

   146	/* ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   147	   3. CONTEXT EXTRACTION
   148	──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */
   149	
   150	function extractContextHint(args: Record<string, unknown> | null | undefined): string | null {
   151	  if (!args || typeof args !== 'object') return null;
   152	
   153	  const contextFields = ['input', 'query', 'prompt', 'specFolder', 'filePath'];
   154	  for (const field of contextFields) {
   155	    if (args[field] && typeof args[field] === 'string' && (args[field] as string).length >= 3) {
   156	      return args[field] as string;
   157	    }
   158	  }
   159	
   160	  // Join concepts array if present
   161	  if (args.concepts && Array.isArray(args.concepts) && args.concepts.length > 0) {
   162	    const strings = args.concepts.filter((c): c is string => typeof c === 'string');
   163	    if (strings.length > 0) return strings.join(' ');
   164	  }
   165	
   166	  return null;
   167	}

   173	async function getConstitutionalMemories(): Promise<ConstitutionalMemory[]> {
   174	  const now = Date.now();
   175	
   176	  if (constitutionalCache && (now - constitutionalCacheTime) < CONSTITUTIONAL_CACHE_TTL) {
   177	    return constitutionalCache;
   178	  }

   186	      FROM memory_index
   187	      WHERE importance_tier = 'constitutional'
   188	      AND embedding_status IN ('success', 'pending', 'partial')
   189	      ORDER BY created_at DESC
   190	      LIMIT 10
   191	    `).all();
   192	
   193	    constitutionalCache = (rows as Record<string, unknown>[]).map((r) => ({
   194	      id: r.id as number,

   198	      importanceTier: r.importance_tier as string
   199	    }));
   200	    constitutionalCacheTime = now;
   201	
   202	    return constitutionalCache;
   203	  } catch (err: unknown) {
   204	    const message = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
   205	    console.warn('[SK-004] Failed to fetch constitutional memories:', message);
   206	    return [];
   207	  }
   208	}

   246	/* ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   247	   5. AUTO-SURFACE MEMORIES
   248	──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */
   249	
   250	function enforceAutoSurfaceTokenBudget(
   251	  result: AutoSurfaceResult | null,
   252	  tokenBudget: number,
   253	  hookName: 'tool-dispatch' | 'compaction' | 'memory-aware'
   254	): AutoSurfaceResult | null {
   255	  if (!result) {
   256	    return null;
   257	  }
   258	
   259	  const measureTokens = (candidate: AutoSurfaceResult): number =>
   260	    estimateTokenCount(JSON.stringify(candidate));
   261	
   262	  const budgetLimit = Number.isFinite(tokenBudget) && tokenBudget > 0
   263	    ? tokenBudget
   264	    : TOOL_DISPATCH_TOKEN_BUDGET;
   265	
   266	  let boundedResult: AutoSurfaceResult = result;
   267	  let tokenCount = measureTokens(boundedResult);
   268	
   269	  if (tokenCount <= budgetLimit) {
   270	    return boundedResult;
   271	  }
   272	
   273	  const triggered = [...boundedResult.triggered];
   274	  while (triggered.length > 0 && tokenCount > budgetLimit) {
   275	    triggered.pop();
   276	    boundedResult = { ...boundedResult, triggered };
   277	    tokenCount = measureTokens(boundedResult);
   278	  }
   279	
   280	  const constitutional = [...boundedResult.constitutional];
   281	  while (constitutional.length > 0 && tokenCount > budgetLimit) {
   282	    constitutional.pop();
   283	    boundedResult = { ...boundedResult, constitutional };
   284	    tokenCount = measureTokens(boundedResult);
   285	  }
   286	
   287	  if (tokenCount > budgetLimit) {
   288	    console.warn(
   289	      `[SK-004] Auto-surface output exceeded ${hookName} token budget ` +
   290	      `(${tokenCount} > ${budgetLimit}); dropping payload`
   291	    );
   292	    return null;
   293	  }
   294	
   295	  console.warn(
   296	    `[SK-004] Auto-surface output truncated to fit ${hookName} token budget ` +
   297	    `(${tokenCount}/${budgetLimit})`
   298	  );
   299	  return boundedResult;
   300	}

   307	 * @param limit - Maximum number of memory IDs to return

   318	    const oneHourAgo = new Date(Date.now() - 60 * 60 * 1000).toISOString();
   319	    const rows = db.prepare(`
   320	      SELECT DISTINCT wm.memory_id

    15	/** Parsed JSON from Claude Code hook stdin */
    16	export interface HookInput {
    17	  readonly session_id?: string;
    18	  readonly transcript_path?: string;
    19	  readonly trigger?: 'auto' | 'manual';
    20	  readonly source?: 'startup' | 'resume' | 'clear' | 'compact';
    21	  readonly custom_instructions?: string;
    22	  readonly stop_hook_active?: boolean;
    23	  readonly last_assistant_message?: string;
    24	  readonly [key: string]: unknown;

    29	  readonly title: string;
    30	  readonly content: string;
    31	}

    33	/** Require a non-empty session_id for any hook that touches shared temp-state. */
    34	export function getRequiredSessionId(sessionId: unknown, surface: string): string {
    35	  const normalized = typeof sessionId === 'string' ? sessionId.trim() : '';
    36	  if (normalized.length === 0) {
    37	    throw new Error(`${surface} hook payload missing required session_id`);
    38	  }
    39	  return normalized;
    40	}
    41	
    42	/** Read and parse JSON from stdin. Returns null on failure. */
    43	export async function parseHookStdin(): Promise<HookInput | null> {
    44	  try {
    45	    const chunks: Buffer[] = [];
    46	    for await (const chunk of process.stdin) {
    47	      chunks.push(chunk as Buffer);
    48	    }
    49	    const raw = Buffer.concat(chunks).toString('utf-8').trim();
    50	    if (!raw) return null;
    51	    return JSON.parse(raw) as HookInput;
    52	  } catch (err: unknown) {
    53	    hookLog('warn', 'stdin', `Failed to parse hook stdin: ${err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err)}`);
    54	    return null;
    55	  }
    56	}
    57	
    58	/** Format sections into readable text block for stdout injection */
    59	export function formatHookOutput(sections: OutputSection[]): string {
    60	  return sections
    61	    .filter(s => s.content.trim().length > 0)
    62	    .map(s => `## ${s.title}\n${s.content}`)
    63	    .join('\n\n');
    64	}
    65	
    66	/** Wrap a promise with a timeout. Returns fallback value on timeout. */
    67	export async function withTimeout<T>(promise: Promise<T>, ms: number, fallback: T): Promise<T> {
    68	  let timer: ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | undefined;
    69	  const timeout = new Promise<T>((resolve) => {
    70	    timer = setTimeout(() => {
    71	      hookLog('warn', 'timeout', `Operation timed out after ${ms}ms`);
    72	      resolve(fallback);
    73	    }, ms);
    74	  });
    75	  try {
    76	    return await Promise.race([promise, timeout]);
    77	  } finally {
    78	    if (timer !== undefined) clearTimeout(timer);
    79	  }
    80	}
    81	
    82	/** Log to stderr (stdout is reserved for hook output injection) */
    83	export function hookLog(level: 'info' | 'warn' | 'error', tag: string, msg: string): void {
    84	  const prefix = `[speckit-hook:${tag}]`;
    85	  const line = `${prefix} ${msg}`;
    86	  if (level === 'error') {
    87	    process.stderr.write(`ERROR ${line}\n`);
    88	  } else if (level === 'warn') {
    89	    process.stderr.write(`WARN ${line}\n`);
    90	  } else {
    91	    process.stderr.write(`INFO ${line}\n`);
    92	  }
    93	}

    95	/** Estimate token count (rough: 1 token ≈ 4 chars) and truncate if over budget */
    96	export function truncateToTokenBudget(text: string, maxTokens: number): string {
    97	  const estimatedTokens = Math.ceil(text.length / 4);
    98	  if (estimatedTokens <= maxTokens) return text;
    99	  const maxChars = maxTokens * 4;
   100	  return text.slice(0, maxChars) + '\n[...truncated to fit token budget]';
   101	}

    28	}

    30	/** Merged compact brief with metadata */
    31	export interface MergedBrief {
    32	  text: string;
    33	  sections: {
    34	    name: string;
    35	    content: string;
    36	    tokenEstimate: number;
    37	    source: string;
    38	  }[];
    39	  allocation: AllocationResult;
    40	  payloadContract: SharedPayloadEnvelope;
    41	  metadata: {
    42	    totalTokenEstimate: number;
    43	    sourceCount: number;
    44	    mergedAt: string;
    45	    mergeDurationMs: number;
    46	    deduplicatedFiles: number;
    47	    freshness: SourceFreshness[];
    48	    selection?: PreMergeSelectionMetadata;
    49	  };
    50	}
    51	
    52	/** Estimate tokens from string (4 chars ≈ 1 token) */
    53	function estimateTokens(text: string): number {
    54	  return Math.ceil(text.length / 4);
    55	}
    56	
    57	/** Truncate text to fit within a token budget */
    58	function truncateToTokens(text: string, maxTokens: number): string {
    59	  if (maxTokens <= 0) return '';
    60	  if (estimateTokens(text) <= maxTokens) return text;
    61	
    62	  const marker = '\n[...truncated]';
    63	  const maxChars = maxTokens * 4;
    64	  if (marker.length >= maxChars) {
    65	    return text.slice(0, maxChars);
    66	  }
    67	
    68	  const contentChars = Math.max(0, maxChars - marker.length);
    69	  return text.slice(0, contentChars) + marker;
    70	}
    71	
    72	/** Extract file paths from a text section for deduplication */
    73	function extractFilePathsFromText(text: string): Set<string> {
    74	  const paths = new Set<string>();
    75	  const pathRegex = /(?:\/[\w.-]+){2,}(?:\.\w+)/g;
    76	  const matches = text.match(pathRegex);
    77	  if (matches) matches.forEach(m => paths.add(m));
    78	  return paths;
    79	}
    80	
    81	/** Deduplicate file references across sections — higher priority sources keep their mentions */
    82	function deduplicateFilePaths(sections: MergedBrief['sections']): number {
    83	  const seenFiles = new Set<string>();
    84	  let removedCount = 0;
    85	
    86	  for (const section of sections) {
    87	    const filePaths = extractFilePathsFromText(section.content);
    88	    const duplicates: string[] = [];
    89	
    90	    for (const fp of filePaths) {
    91	      if (seenFiles.has(fp)) {
    92	        duplicates.push(fp);
    93	        removedCount++;
    94	      } else {
    95	        seenFiles.add(fp);
    96	      }
    97	    }
    98	
    99	    // Remove duplicate file path lines from lower-priority sections
   100	    if (duplicates.length > 0) {
   101	      let content = section.content;
   102	      for (const dup of duplicates) {
   103	        const lineRegex = new RegExp(`^.*${dup.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&')}.*$\n?`, 'gm');
   104	        content = content.replace(lineRegex, '');
   105	      }
   106	      section.content = content.trim();
   107	      section.tokenEstimate = estimateTokens(section.content);
   108	    }
   109	  }
   110	  return removedCount;
   111	}
   112	
   113	/**
   114	 * Merge context from multiple sources into a compact brief.
   115	 *
   116	 * Strategy:
   117	 * 1. Allocate budget across sources (floor + overflow)
   118	 * 2. Truncate each source to its granted budget
   119	 * 3. Deduplicate at file level (same file from multiple sources → keep highest priority)
   120	 * 4. Render sections in priority order with headers
   121	 */
   122	export function mergeCompactBrief(
   123	  input: MergeInput,
   124	  totalBudget: number = 4000,
   125	  freshness?: SourceFreshness[],
   126	  selection?: PreMergeSelectionMetadata,
   127	): MergedBrief {
   128	  const startTime = performance.now();
   129	
   130	  const constitutionalSize = estimateTokens(input.constitutional);
   131	  const codeGraphSize = estimateTokens(input.codeGraph);
   132	  const cocoIndexSize = estimateTokens(input.cocoIndex);
   133	  const triggeredSize = estimateTokens(input.triggered);
   134	  const sessionStateSize = estimateTokens(input.sessionState);
   135	
   136	  const sources = createDefaultSources(
   137	    constitutionalSize,
   138	    codeGraphSize,
   139	    cocoIndexSize,
   140	    triggeredSize,
   141	    sessionStateSize,
   142	  );
   143	  const allocation = allocateBudget(sources, totalBudget);
   144	
   145	  // Build sections with granted budgets
   146	  const sections: MergedBrief['sections'] = [];
   147	  const allocationMap = new Map(allocation.allocations.map(a => [a.name, a]));
   148	  const pushSection = (
   149	    inputText: string,
   150	    allocationName: string,
   151	    sectionName: string,
   152	    source: string,
   153	  ): void => {
   154	    if (!inputText.trim()) return;
   155	
   156	    const granted = allocationMap.get(allocationName)?.granted ?? 0;
   157	    if (granted <= 0) return;
   158	
   159	    const content = truncateToTokens(inputText, granted);
   160	    if (!content.trim()) return;
   161	
   162	    sections.push({
   163	      name: sectionName,
   164	      content,
   165	      tokenEstimate: estimateTokens(content),
   166	      source,
   167	    });
   168	  };
   169	
   170	  pushSection(input.constitutional, 'constitutional', 'Constitutional Rules', 'memory');
   171	  pushSection(input.codeGraph, 'codeGraph', 'Active Files & Structural Context', 'code-graph');
   172	  pushSection(input.cocoIndex, 'cocoIndex', 'Semantic Neighbors', 'cocoindex');
   173	  pushSection(input.sessionState, 'sessionState', 'Session State / Next Steps', 'session');
   174	  pushSection(input.triggered, 'triggered', 'Triggered Memories', 'memory');
   175	
   176	  // File-level deduplication across sections
   177	  const deduplicatedFiles = deduplicateFilePaths(sections);
   178	
   179	  // Render final text
   180	  const text = sections

   500	function resolveSubjectToRef(subject: string): ArtifactRef | null {
   501	  try {
   502	    const d = graphDb.getDb();

   507	      LIMIT 1
   508	    `).get(subject, subject, subject) as Record<string, unknown> | undefined;

   530	/**
   531	 * Format sections into compact text brief within token budget.
   532	 * Never-drops guarantee: always includes top seed, root anchor, one boundary edge, one next action.
   533	 */
   534	function formatTextBrief(sections: GraphContextSection[], budgetTokens: number, _anchors?: ArtifactRef[]): FormattedTextBrief {
   535	  const maxChars = budgetTokens * 4;
   536	  const lines: string[] = [];
   537	  let omittedSections = 0;
   538	
   539	  // Priority rendering: first section is always fully rendered (never dropped)
   540	  for (let i = 0; i < sections.length; i++) {
   541	    const section = sections[i];
   542	    const isFirst = i === 0;
   543	    const nodeLimit = isFirst ? 15 : Math.max(5, 15 - i * 3);
   544	    const edgeLimit = isFirst ? 10 : Math.max(3, 10 - i * 2);
   545	
   546	    lines.push(`### ${section.anchor}`);
   547	
   548	    if (section.nodes.length > 0) {
   549	      lines.push('Symbols:');
   550	      for (const n of section.nodes.slice(0, nodeLimit)) {
   551	        lines.push(`  ${n.kind} ${n.name} (${n.file}:${n.line})`);
   552	      }
   553	      if (section.nodes.length > nodeLimit) {
   554	        lines.push(`  ... +${section.nodes.length - nodeLimit} more`);
   555	      }
   556	    }
   557	
   558	    if (section.edges.length > 0) {
   559	      lines.push('Relationships:');
   560	      for (const e of section.edges.slice(0, edgeLimit)) {
   561	        const metadata = [
   562	          e.reason ? `reason=${e.reason}` : null,
   563	          e.step ? `step=${e.step}` : null,
   564	          typeof e.confidence === 'number' ? `confidence=${e.confidence}` : null,
   565	        ].filter(Boolean).join(' ');
   566	        lines.push(`  ${e.from} -[${e.type}${metadata ? ` ${metadata}` : ''}]-> ${e.to}`);
   567	      }
   568	      if (section.edges.length > edgeLimit) {
   569	        lines.push(`  ... +${section.edges.length - edgeLimit} more`);
   570	      }
   571	    }
   572	
   573	    lines.push('');
   574	
   575	    // Budget check: stop adding sections if we're over budget (but first section always included)
   576	    if (!isFirst && lines.join('\n').length > maxChars * 0.9) {
   577	      omittedSections = sections.length - i - 1;
   578	      lines.push(`[${omittedSections} more sections omitted — budget limit]`);
   579	      break;
   580	    }
   581	  }
   582	
   583	  let result = lines.join('\n');
   584	  let truncated = false;
   585	  if (result.length > maxChars) {
   586	    truncated = true;
   587	    result = result.slice(0, maxChars) + '\n[...truncated]';
   588	  }
   589	  return {
   590	    text: result,
   591	    omittedSections,
   592	    truncated,
   593	  };
   594	}

    42	const MIN_TOTAL_MEMORY_BYTES = 8 * 1024 * 1024 * 1024;
    43	// Lower total-memory threshold when custom model is configured — still
    44	// Prevents OOM on truly constrained systems without blocking intentional
    45	// Overrides. We use totalmem() because freemem() is unreliable on macOS/Linux
    46	// Where disk cache can make "free" memory appear deceptively low.
    47	const MIN_TOTAL_MEMORY_CUSTOM_BYTES = 2 * 1024 * 1024 * 1024;
    48	const DEFAULT_MODEL_RELATIVE_PATH = path.join('models', 'bge-reranker-v2-m3.Q4_K_M.gguf');
    49	const RERANKER_TIMEOUT_MS = Number(process.env.SPECKIT_RERANKER_TIMEOUT_MS) || 30_000;
    50	const MAX_PROMPT_BYTES = 10 * 1024;
    51	const MAX_RERANK_CANDIDATES = 50;

    53	/* ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    54	   4. MODEL MANAGEMENT
    55	──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */
    56	
    57	let cachedLlama: unknown | null = null;
    58	let cachedModel: unknown | null = null;
    59	let cachedModelPath: string | null = null;
    60	let modelLoadPromise: Promise<unknown> | null = null;
    61	let modelLoadPromisePath: string | null = null;
    62	
    63	function resolveModelPath(): string {
    64	  const configured = process.env.SPECKIT_RERANKER_MODEL?.trim();
    65	  if (!configured) {
    66	    return path.resolve(process.cwd(), DEFAULT_MODEL_RELATIVE_PATH);
    67	  }
    68	  if (path.isAbsolute(configured)) {
    69	    return configured;
    70	  }
    71	  return path.resolve(process.cwd(), configured);
    72	}

    74	function resolveRowText(row: LocalRerankRow): string {
    75	  if (typeof row.content === 'string' && row.content.trim().length > 0) {
    76	    return row.content.trim();
    77	  }
    78	  if (typeof row.file_path === 'string' && row.file_path.trim().length > 0) {
    79	    return row.file_path.trim();
    80	  }
    81	  return '';
    82	}
    83	
    84	async function loadNodeLlamaCpp(): Promise<NodeLlamaCppModule> {
    85	  const dynamicImport = new Function('m', 'return import(m)');
    86	  const mod = await dynamicImport('node-llama-cpp') as unknown;
    87	  if (!mod || typeof mod !== 'object' || typeof (mod as NodeLlamaCppModule).getLlama !== 'function') {
    88	    throw new Error('node-llama-cpp loaded without getLlama() export');
    89	  }
    90	  return mod as NodeLlamaCppModule;
    91	}
    92	
    93	async function ensureModelLoaded(modelPath: string): Promise<unknown> {
    94	  // Fast path: model already cached for this path
    95	  if (cachedModel && cachedModelPath === modelPath) {
    96	    return cachedModel;
    97	  }
    98	
    99	  // H4 fix: Explicitly reuse in-flight promise for the same model path
   100	  // To prevent concurrent callers from orphaning promises
   101	  if (modelLoadPromise && modelLoadPromisePath === modelPath) {
   102	    return await modelLoadPromise;
   103	  }
   104	
   105	  // Discard stale promise if the model path changed since the last load
   106	  if (modelLoadPromise && modelLoadPromisePath !== modelPath) {
   107	    modelLoadPromise = null;
   108	    modelLoadPromisePath = null;
   109	  }
   110	
   111	  modelLoadPromisePath = modelPath;
   112	  modelLoadPromise = (async () => {
   113	    const llamaModule = await loadNodeLlamaCpp();
   114	    cachedLlama = await llamaModule.getLlama();
   115	    if (!cachedLlama || typeof cachedLlama !== 'object') {
   116	      throw new Error('getLlama() did not return a usable object');
   117	    }
   118	    const loadModel = (cachedLlama as { loadModel?: (args: { modelPath: string }) => Promise<unknown> }).loadModel;
   119	    if (typeof loadModel !== 'function') {
   120	      throw new Error('node-llama-cpp runtime missing loadModel()');
   121	    }
   122	    const model = await loadModel.call(cachedLlama, { modelPath });
   123	    if (!model || typeof model !== 'object') {
   124	      throw new Error('loadModel() returned invalid model');
   125	    }
   126	    cachedModel = model;
   127	    cachedModelPath = modelPath;
   128	    return model;
   129	  })();
   130	
   131	  try {
   132	    return await modelLoadPromise;
   133	  } catch (error: unknown) {
   134	    modelLoadPromise = null;
   135	    modelLoadPromisePath = null;
   136	    cachedModel = null;
   137	    cachedModelPath = null;
   138	    throw error;
   139	  }
   140	}
   141	
   142	/* ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   143	   5. SCORING
   144	──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */
   145	
   146	function normalizeScore(value: number): number {
   147	  if (!Number.isFinite(value)) return 0;
   148	  // Keep score bounded and monotonic without assuming provider-native scale.
   149	  return (Math.tanh(value) + 1) / 2;
   150	}
   151	
   152	function extractNumericScore(value: unknown): number | null {
   153	  if (typeof value === 'number' && Number.isFinite(value)) {
   154	    return value;
   155	  }
   156	  if (typeof value === 'string') {
   157	    const parsed = Number.parseFloat(value);
   158	    return Number.isFinite(parsed) ? parsed : null;
   159	  }
   160	  if (value && typeof value === 'object') {
   161	    const record = value as Record<string, unknown>;
   162	    const directKeys = ['score', 'relevance', 'relevanceScore', 'similarity', 'logit'];
   163	    for (const key of directKeys) {
   164	      const extracted = extractNumericScore(record[key]);
   165	      if (extracted !== null) return extracted;
   166	    }
   167	  }
   168	  return null;
   169	}
   170	
   171	async function scorePrompt(context: unknown, prompt: string): Promise<number> {
   172	  if (!context || typeof context !== 'object') {
   173	    throw new Error('Invalid llama context');
   174	  }
   175	
   176	  const directFns = ['score', 'getScore', 'evaluate', 'eval'] as const;
   177	  for (const fnName of directFns) {
   178	    const fn = (context as Record<string, unknown>)[fnName];
   179	    if (typeof fn === 'function') {
   180	      const raw = await (fn as (input: string) => Promise<unknown>).call(context, prompt);
   181	      const score = extractNumericScore(raw);
   182	      if (score !== null) return normalizeScore(score);
   183	    }
   184	  }
   185	
   186	  const getSequence = (context as { getSequence?: () => Promise<unknown> }).getSequence;
   187	  if (typeof getSequence === 'function') {
   188	    const sequence = await getSequence.call(context);
   189	    if (sequence && typeof sequence === 'object') {
   190	      const seqEval = (sequence as { evaluate?: (input: string) => Promise<unknown> }).evaluate;
   191	      if (typeof seqEval === 'function') {
   192	        const raw = await seqEval.call(sequence, prompt);
   193	        const score = extractNumericScore(raw);
   194	        if (score !== null) return normalizeScore(score);
   195	      }
   196	    }
   197	  }
   198	
   199	  throw new Error('Unable to resolve a scoring method from llama context');
   200	}
