   202	/* ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   203	   6. PUBLIC API
   204	──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */
   205	
   206	/**
   207	 * Feature-flag gate for local reranking.
   208	 * This guard is intentionally strict: local reranking only runs when the
   209	 * operator opts in with `RERANKER_LOCAL=true`, has enough total RAM, and the
   210	 * configured GGUF model file is available.
   211	 */
   212	export async function canUseLocalReranker(): Promise<boolean> {
   213	  if (process.env.RERANKER_LOCAL?.toLowerCase().trim() !== 'true') {
   214	    return false;
   215	  }
   216	
   217	  // Use total system memory instead of free memory. On macOS/Linux,
   218	  // Os.freemem() can look artificially low due to disk cache usage.
   219	  const hasCustomModel = Boolean(process.env.SPECKIT_RERANKER_MODEL?.trim());
   220	  const memThreshold = hasCustomModel ? MIN_TOTAL_MEMORY_CUSTOM_BYTES : MIN_TOTAL_MEMORY_BYTES;
   221	  if (os.totalmem() < memThreshold) {
   222	    return false;
   223	  }
   224	
   225	  const modelPath = resolveModelPath();
   226	  try {
   227	    await access(modelPath);
   228	    return true;
   229	  } catch (_error: unknown) {
   230	    return false;
   231	  }
   232	}
   233	
   234	/**
   235	 * Local GGUF reranking entrypoint for Stage 3.
   236	 * Falls back to original ordering whenever preconditions fail or runtime
   237	 * inference errors occur, preserving deterministic behavior.
   238	 */
   239	export async function rerankLocal<T extends LocalRerankRow>(
   240	  query: string,
   241	  candidates: T[],
   242	  topK: number
   243	): Promise<T[]> {
   244	  if (!Array.isArray(candidates) || candidates.length < 2) {
   245	    return candidates;
   246	  }
   247	
   248	  /**
   249	   * Internal guard for direct callers: rerankLocal re-checks eligibility even
   250	   * when invoked outside the Stage 3 flag path, and fails closed to the
   251	   * original ranking when local execution is unavailable.
   252	   */
   253	  const localEnabled = await canUseLocalReranker();
   254	  if (!localEnabled) {
   255	    return candidates;
   256	  }
   257	
   258	  const modelPath = resolveModelPath();
   259	  const rerankCandidates = candidates.slice(0, MAX_RERANK_CANDIDATES);
   260	  const rerankCount = Math.max(1, Math.min(topK, rerankCandidates.length));
   261	  const startedAt = Date.now();
   262	
   263	  let context: unknown | null = null;
   264	  let timeoutId: ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | null = null;
   265	  try {
   266	    const model = await ensureModelLoaded(modelPath);
   267	    const createContext = (model as { createContext?: () => Promise<unknown> }).createContext;
   268	    if (typeof createContext !== 'function') {
   269	      throw new Error('Loaded model does not expose createContext()');
   270	    }
   271	    context = await createContext.call(model);
   272	
   273	    /**
   274	     * Feature-flagged local inference branch.
   275	     * This code path exists for opt-in deployments (`RERANKER_LOCAL=true`) so
   276	     * local GGUF reranking can be exercised without changing the default
   277	     * remote/fallback behavior for non-opted-in environments.
   278	     *
   279	     * [CHK-069] Quality comparison against Cohere/Voyage is deferred to
   280	     * `tests/reranker-eval-comparison.vitest.ts`, where benchmark protocol and
   281	     * remote-provider requirements are isolated from runtime code paths.
   282	     */
   283	    const reranked = await Promise.race([
   284	      (async (): Promise<T[]> => {
   285	        // Sequential scoring instead of Promise.all to avoid
   286	        // Allocating multiple sequence states simultaneously in VRAM, which
   287	        // Can trigger OOM or context mixing on local LLM inference.
   288	        // PERF(CHK-113): Sequential per-candidate inference. For 20 candidates, latency depends on
   289	        // Model size and hardware. On Apple Silicon with small GGUF (~100MB), expect 200-400ms.
   290	        // Future optimization: batch inference via node-llama-cpp's evaluateBatch API.
   291	        const scored: Array<{ candidate: T; rerankScore: number }> = [];
   292	        for (const candidate of rerankCandidates.slice(0, rerankCount)) {
   293	          const content = resolveRowText(candidate);
   294	          const prompt = `query: ${query}\ndocument: ${content}`;
   295	          // Truncate by character count after converting from bytes to avoid
   296	          // Splitting multi-byte UTF-8 sequences (which produces replacement chars).
   297	          let boundedPrompt = prompt;
   298	          if (Buffer.byteLength(prompt, 'utf8') > MAX_PROMPT_BYTES) {
   299	            const buf = Buffer.from(prompt, 'utf8');
   300	            let end = MAX_PROMPT_BYTES;
   301	            // Walk back to a valid UTF-8 boundary (continuation bytes start with 10xxxxxx).
   302	            while (end > 0 && (buf[end] & 0xC0) === 0x80) { end -= 1; }
   303	            boundedPrompt = buf.subarray(0, end).toString('utf8');
   304	          }
   305	          const rerankScore = await scorePrompt(context, boundedPrompt);
   306	          scored.push({ candidate, rerankScore });
   307	        }
   308	
   309	        scored.sort((a, b) => b.rerankScore - a.rerankScore);
   310	        const rerankedTop = scored.map((entry) => ({
   311	          ...entry.candidate,
   312	          rerankerScore: entry.rerankScore,
   313	          score: entry.rerankScore,
   314	        }));
   315	        const remainder = candidates.slice(rerankCount);
   316	        const elapsed = Date.now() - startedAt;
   317	        console.error(
   318	          `[local-reranker] reranked=${rerankCount} total=${candidates.length} durationMs=${elapsed} model=${path.basename(modelPath)}`
   319	        );
   320	        return [...rerankedTop, ...remainder];
   321	      })(),
   322	      new Promise<never>((_, reject) => {
   323	        timeoutId = setTimeout(() => {
   324	          reject(new Error(`local reranker timed out after ${RERANKER_TIMEOUT_MS}ms`));
   325	        }, RERANKER_TIMEOUT_MS);

 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
     2	// MODULE: Budget Allocator
     3	// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
     4	// Distributes a total token budget across multiple context sources
     5	// using floor allocations + overflow redistribution.
     6	
     7	/** Per-source budget configuration */
     8	export interface SourceBudget {
     9	  name: string;
    10	  floor: number;
    11	  actualSize: number; // 0 if source is empty
    12	}
    13	
    14	/** Allocation result for a single source */
    15	export interface SourceAllocation {
    16	  name: string;
    17	  floor: number;
    18	  requested: number;
    19	  granted: number;
    20	  dropped: number;
    21	}
    22	
    23	/** Combined allocation result */
    24	export interface AllocationResult {
    25	  totalBudget: number;
    26	  totalUsed: number;
    27	  overflow: number;
    28	  allocations: SourceAllocation[];
    29	}
    30	
    31	/** Default floor layout for the 4000-token compact brief budget */
    32	export const DEFAULT_FLOORS = {
    33	  constitutional: 700,
    34	  codeGraph: 1200,
    35	  cocoIndex: 900,
    36	  triggered: 400,
    37	  overflow: 800,
    38	} as const;
    39	
    40	/** Priority order for overflow redistribution (highest first) */
    41	const PRIORITY_ORDER = ['constitutional', 'codeGraph', 'cocoIndex', 'sessionState', 'triggered'] as const;
    42	
    43	/**
    44	 * Allocate token budget across sources.
    45	 *
    46	 * Algorithm:
    47	 * 1. Assign floor to each source (capped at actual size)
    48	 * 2. Calculate overflow from empty/under-floor sources
    49	 * 3. Redistribute overflow by priority order
    50	 * 4. Enforce total budget cap with deterministic trim
    51	 */
    52	export function allocateBudget(
    53	  sources: SourceBudget[],
    54	  totalBudget: number = 4000,
    55	): AllocationResult {
    56	  const allocations: SourceAllocation[] = [];
    57	  const floorTotal = sources.reduce((sum, source) => sum + source.floor, 0);
    58	  let overflowPool = Math.max(totalBudget - floorTotal, 0);
    59	
    60	  // Step 1: Assign floors, collect overflow from empty sources
    61	  for (const source of sources) {
    62	    const floor = source.floor;
    63	    const granted = Math.min(floor, source.actualSize);
    64	    const unused = floor - granted;
    65	    overflowPool += unused;
    66	
    67	    allocations.push({
    68	      name: source.name,
    69	      floor,
    70	      requested: source.actualSize,
    71	      granted,
    72	      dropped: Math.max(0, source.actualSize - granted),
    73	    });
    74	  }
    75	
    76	  // Step 2: Redistribute overflow by priority
    77	  if (overflowPool > 0) {
    78	    for (const priorityName of PRIORITY_ORDER) {
    79	      const alloc = allocations.find(a => a.name === priorityName);
    80	      if (!alloc) continue;
    81	
    82	      const headroom = alloc.requested - alloc.granted;
    83	      if (headroom <= 0) continue;
    84	
    85	      const bonus = Math.min(headroom, overflowPool);
    86	      alloc.granted += bonus;
    87	      alloc.dropped -= bonus;
    88	      overflowPool -= bonus;
    89	
    90	      if (overflowPool <= 0) break;
    91	    }
    92	  }
    93	
    94	  // Step 3: Enforce total budget cap (trim in reverse priority order)
    95	  let totalUsed = allocations.reduce((sum, a) => sum + a.granted, 0);
    96	  if (totalUsed > totalBudget) {
    97	    const reversed = [...PRIORITY_ORDER].reverse();
    98	    for (const name of reversed) {
    99	      if (totalUsed <= totalBudget) break;
   100	      const alloc = allocations.find(a => a.name === name);
   101	      if (!alloc) continue;
   102	
   103	      const excess = totalUsed - totalBudget;
   104	      const trim = Math.min(excess, alloc.granted);
   105	      alloc.granted -= trim;
   106	      alloc.dropped += trim;
   107	      totalUsed -= trim;
   108	    }
   109	  }
   110	
   111	  return {
   112	    totalBudget,
   113	    totalUsed: allocations.reduce((sum, a) => sum + a.granted, 0),
   114	    overflow: overflowPool,
   115	    allocations,
   116	  };
   117	}
   118	
   119	/** Create source budgets with default floors */
   120	export function createDefaultSources(
   121	  constitutionalSize: number,
   122	  codeGraphSize: number,
   123	  cocoIndexSize: number,
   124	  triggeredSize: number,
   125	  sessionStateSize: number = 0,
   126	): SourceBudget[] {
   127	  return [
   128	    { name: 'constitutional', floor: DEFAULT_FLOORS.constitutional, actualSize: constitutionalSize },
   129	    { name: 'codeGraph', floor: DEFAULT_FLOORS.codeGraph, actualSize: codeGraphSize },
   130	    { name: 'cocoIndex', floor: DEFAULT_FLOORS.cocoIndex, actualSize: cocoIndexSize },
   131	    { name: 'sessionState', floor: 0, actualSize: sessionStateSize },
   132	    { name: 'triggered', floor: DEFAULT_FLOORS.triggered, actualSize: triggeredSize },
   133	  ];
   134	}

   222	interface ResumeRow extends Record<string, unknown> {
   223	  id: string;
   224	  title: string;
   225	  filePath: string;
   226	  specFolder: string;
   227	  documentType: 'handover' | 'continuity' | 'spec_doc';
   228	  source: 'handover' | 'continuity' | 'spec_docs';
   229	  score: number;
   230	  similarity: number;
   231	  fingerprint: string;
   232	  fingerprintExpected: string | null;
   233	  fingerprintStatus: 'verified';
   234	  content: string;
   235	}

   237	const RESUME_LADDER_ORDER = ['handover', 'continuity', 'spec_docs'] as const;
   238	
   239	const STRUCTURAL_ROUTING_PATTERNS = [
   240	  /\b(?:who|what)\s+calls?\b/i,
   241	  /\bcallers?\s+of\b/i,
   242	  /\b(?:who|what)\s+imports?\b/i,
   243	  /\bimports?\s+of\b/i,
   244	  /\b(?:show|list)\s+(?:the\s+)?outline\b/i,
   245	  /\boutline\s+of\b/i,
   246	  /\bdependenc(?:y|ies)\b/i,
   247	  /\bdependents?\b/i,
   248	  /\bwhat\s+extends\b/i,
   249	];

   251	function extractResultRowsFromContextResponse(responseText: string): Array<Record<string, unknown>> {
   252	  try {
   253	    const parsed = JSON.parse(responseText) as Record<string, unknown>;
   254	    const outerData = parsed?.data as Record<string, unknown> | undefined;
   255	
   256	    const directRows = Array.isArray(outerData?.results)
   257	      ? outerData.results as Array<Record<string, unknown>>
   258	      : null;
   259	    if (directRows) {
   260	      return directRows;
   261	    }
   262	
   263	    const nestedContent = Array.isArray(outerData?.content)
   264	      ? outerData.content as Array<{ type?: string; text?: string }>
   265	      : [];
   266	    const nestedText = nestedContent[0]?.text;
   267	    if (typeof nestedText !== 'string' || nestedText.length === 0) {
   268	      return [];
   269	    }
   270	
   271	    const nestedEnvelope = JSON.parse(nestedText) as Record<string, unknown>;
   272	    const nestedData = nestedEnvelope?.data as Record<string, unknown> | undefined;
   273	    return Array.isArray(nestedData?.results)
   274	      ? nestedData.results as Array<Record<string, unknown>>
   275	      : [];
   276	  } catch {
   277	    return [];
   278	  }
   279	}
   280	
   281	function readResumeDocumentContent(documentPath: string): string {
   282	  try {
   283	    return readFileSync(documentPath, 'utf8');
   284	  } catch {
   285	    return '';
   286	  }
   287	}
   288	
   289	function formatResumeLadderContent(result: ResumeLadderResult, row: ResumeRow): string {
   290	  if (row.documentType !== 'continuity') {
   291	    return readResumeDocumentContent(row.filePath);
   292	  }
   293	
   294	  const lines = [
   295	    `Recent action: ${result.recentAction ?? ''}`,
   296	    `Next safe action: ${result.nextSafeAction ?? ''}`,
   297	  ];
   298	
   299	  if (result.blockers.length > 0) {
   300	    lines.push(`Blockers: ${result.blockers.join('; ')}`);
   301	  }
   302	  if (result.keyFiles.length > 0) {
   303	    lines.push(`Key files: ${result.keyFiles.join(', ')}`);
   304	  }
   305	
   306	  return lines.join('\n');
   307	}
   308	
   309	function normalizeResumeSource(
   310	  source: ResumeLadderResult['source'],
   311	): 'handover' | 'continuity' | 'spec_docs' | 'unresolved' {
   312	  if (source === 'spec-docs') {
   313	    return 'spec_docs';
   314	  }
   315	  if (source === 'none') {
   316	    return 'unresolved';
   317	  }
   318	  return source;
   319	}
   320	
   321	function normalizeResumeDocumentType(
   322	  type: ResumeLadderResult['documents'][number]['type'],
   323	): ResumeRow['documentType'] {
   324	  if (type === 'spec-doc') {
   325	    return 'spec_doc';
   326	  }
   327	  return type;
   328	}
   329	
   330	function convertResumeLadderToRows(result: ResumeLadderResult, limit: number): ResumeRow[] {
   331	  const preferredDocuments = result.documents.filter((document) => {
   332	    if (result.source === 'handover') {
   333	      return document.type === 'handover';
   334	    }
   335	    if (result.source === 'continuity') {
   336	      return document.type === 'continuity';
   337	    }
   338	    if (result.source === 'spec-docs') {
   339	      return document.type === 'spec-doc';
   340	    }
   341	    return false;
   342	  });
   343	
   344	  return preferredDocuments.slice(0, limit).map((document) => {
   345	    const documentType = normalizeResumeDocumentType(document.type);
   346	    const source = normalizeResumeSource(result.source === 'none' ? 'spec-docs' : result.source) as ResumeRow['source'];
   347	    const row: ResumeRow = {
   348	      id: `resume:${source}:${document.relativePath}`,
   349	      title: document.relativePath,
   350	      filePath: document.path,
   351	      specFolder: result.specFolder ?? '',
   352	      documentType,
   353	      source,
   354	      score: 1,
   355	      similarity: 1,
   356	      fingerprint: document.fingerprint,
   357	      fingerprintExpected: null,
   358	      fingerprintStatus: 'verified',
   359	      content: '',
   360	    };
   361	
   362	    row.content = formatResumeLadderContent(result, row);
   363	    return row;
   364	  });
   365	}
   366	
   367	function extractStrategyError(result: ContextResult): StrategyErrorPayload | null {
   368	  if ((result as Record<string, unknown>).isError !== true) {
   369	    return null;
   370	  }
   371	
   372	  const content = Array.isArray((result as Record<string, unknown>).content)
   373	    ? ((result as Record<string, unknown>).content as Array<{ text?: string }>)
   374	    : [];
   375	  const responseText = content[0]?.text;
   376	  if (typeof responseText !== 'string' || responseText.length === 0) {
   377	    return {
   378	      error: 'Context strategy failed',
   379	      code: 'E_STRATEGY',
   380	      details: {},
   381	      hints: [],
   382	      severity: null,
   383	    };
   384	  }
   385	
   386	  try {
   387	    const parsed = JSON.parse(responseText) as {
   388	      data?: {
   389	        error?: string;
   390	        code?: string;
   391	        details?: Record<string, unknown>;
   392	      };
   393	      hints?: string[];
   394	      meta?: {
   395	        severity?: string;
   396	      };
   397	    };
   398	
   399	    return {
   400	      error: parsed.data?.error ?? 'Context strategy failed',
   401	      code: parsed.data?.code ?? 'E_STRATEGY',
   402	      details: parsed.data?.details ?? {},
   403	      hints: Array.isArray(parsed.hints) ? parsed.hints : [],
   404	      severity: parsed.meta?.severity ?? null,
   405	    };
   406	  } catch {
   407	    return {
   408	      error: 'Context strategy failed',
   409	      code: 'E_STRATEGY',
   410	      details: {},
   411	      hints: [],
   412	      severity: null,
   413	    };
   414	  }
   415	}
   416	
   417	function buildStructuralRoutingNudge(
   418	  input: string,
   419	  queryIntentMetadata: {
   420	    queryIntent: string;
   421	    confidence: number;
   422	  } | null,
   423	  graphContextResult: Record<string, unknown> | null,
   424	): StructuralRoutingNudgeMeta | null {
   425	  if (!queryIntentMetadata || queryIntentMetadata.queryIntent !== 'structural' || queryIntentMetadata.confidence <= 0.65) {
   426	    return null;
   427	  }
   428	
   429	  if (!STRUCTURAL_ROUTING_PATTERNS.some((pattern) => pattern.test(input))) {
   430	    return null;
   431	  }
   432	
   433	  const metadata = graphContextResult?.metadata as Record<string, unknown> | undefined;
   434	  const totalNodes = typeof metadata?.totalNodes === 'number' ? metadata.totalNodes : 0;
   435	  if (totalNodes <= 0) {
   436	    return null;
   437	  }
   438	
   439	  return {
   440	    advisory: true,
   441	    advisoryPreset: 'ready',
   442	    preferredTool: 'code_graph_query',
   443	    message: 'Advisory only: this looks like a structural question. Prefer `code_graph_query` before Grep or Glob for callers, imports, outline, and dependency lookups.',
   444	    preservesAuthority: 'session_bootstrap',
   445	  };
   446	}
   447	
   448	/* ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   449	   2. TOKEN BUDGET ENFORCEMENT (T205)
   450	   
   451	   Enforces per-layer/per-mode token budgets by estimating the
   452	   token count of strategy results and truncating when exceeded.
   453	   Uses character-based estimation: 1 token ≈ 4 chars.
   454	──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */
   455	
   456	/**
   457	 * T205: Enforce token budget on strategy results.
   458	 * 
   459	 * Estimates the token count of the serialized result. If over budget,
   460	 * parses embedded result arrays and removes lowest-priority items
   461	 * until within budget. Higher-scored results are preserved.
   462	 */
   463	function enforceTokenBudget(result: ContextResult, budgetTokens: number): { result: ContextResult; enforcement: TokenBudgetEnforcement } {
   464	  const serialized = JSON.stringify(result);
   465	  const preEnforcementTokens = estimateTokens(serialized);
   466	
   467	  // Under budget — no enforcement needed
   468	  if (preEnforcementTokens <= budgetTokens) {
   469	    return {
   470	      result,
   471	      enforcement: {
   472	        budgetTokens,
   473	        preEnforcementTokens,
   474	        returnedTokens: preEnforcementTokens,
   475	        actualTokens: preEnforcementTokens,
   476	        enforced: false,
   477	        truncated: false,
   478	      }
   479	    };
   480	  }
   481	
   482	  // REQ-002 (Cluster 1) Sanity guard: when reported usage is far below budget but
   483	  // we somehow entered enforcement (e.g. estimator ran twice on already-truncated
   484	  // payload, or budget was passed in as a tiny number), short-circuit and return
   485	  // the unmodified result. This prevents the historical regression where a
   486	  // 71-token payload against a 3000-token budget was nuked to count:0,results:[].
   487	  if (budgetTokens > 0 && preEnforcementTokens / budgetTokens < 0.50) {
   488	    return {
   489	      result,
   490	      enforcement: {
   491	        budgetTokens,
   492	        preEnforcementTokens,
   493	        returnedTokens: preEnforcementTokens,
   494	        actualTokens: preEnforcementTokens,
   495	        enforced: false,
   496	        truncated: false,
   497	      }
   498	    };
   499	  }
   500	
   501	  // Over budget — attempt to truncate embedded results
   502	  // Strategy results contain an embedded MCPResponse with content[0].text as JSON
   503	  // That JSON has a .data.results array we can truncate
   504	  const truncatedResult = { ...result };
   505	  let parseFailed = false;
   506	  let originalResultCount: number | undefined;
   507	  let returnedResultCount: number | undefined;
   508	  let droppedAllResultsReason: DroppedAllResultsReason | undefined;
   509	
   510	  const extractNestedResultCount = (candidate: ContextResult): number | undefined => {
   511	    try {
   512	      const candidateContent = (candidate as Record<string, unknown>).content as Array<{ text?: string }> | undefined;
   513	      if (!candidateContent?.[0]?.text) {
   514	        return undefined;
   515	      }
   516	      const parsed = JSON.parse(candidateContent[0].text) as { data?: { results?: unknown[] } };
   517	      return Array.isArray(parsed?.data?.results) ? parsed.data.results.length : undefined;
   518	    } catch {
   519	      return undefined;
   520	    }

exec

 succeeded in 0ms:
   520	    }
   521	  };
   522	
   523	  const fallbackToStructuredBudget = (
   524	    baseResult: ContextResult,
   525	    parseFailedInnerText?: string,
   526	    preservedResults?: Array<Record<string, unknown>>,
   527	  ): ContextResult => {
   528	    const fallbackResult = { ...baseResult } as ContextResult;
   529	    const fallbackContent = Array.isArray((fallbackResult as Record<string, unknown>).content)
   530	      ? ((fallbackResult as Record<string, unknown>).content as Array<Record<string, unknown>>)
   531	      : [];
   532	    const contentClone = fallbackContent.map((entry) => ({ ...entry }));
   533	
   534	    // REQ-002 (Cluster 1): When structural truncation already produced a non-empty
   535	    // result set, preserve it rather than silently dropping to count:0,results:[].
   536	    // The previous behaviour caused the wrapper to report `returnedResultCount > 0`
   537	    // in metadata while shipping an empty payload to the caller.
   538	    const preservedSafe: Array<Record<string, unknown>> = Array.isArray(preservedResults)
   539	      ? preservedResults
   540	      : [];
   541	
   542	    const buildPreservedCandidates = (): Array<Record<string, unknown>> => {
   543	      if (preservedSafe.length === 0) {
   544	        return [];
   545	      }
   546	      const minimalResults = preservedSafe.map((r) => ({
   547	        id: r.id,
   548	        title: r.title,
   549	        similarity: r.similarity,
   550	        specFolder: r.specFolder,
   551	        confidence: r.confidence,
   552	        importanceTier: r.importanceTier,
   553	        isConstitutional: r.isConstitutional,
   554	        metadataOnly: true,
   555	      }));
   556	      return [
   557	        {
   558	          summary: 'Context truncated to fit token budget',
   559	          data: {
   560	            count: preservedSafe.length,
   561	            results: preservedSafe,
   562	          },
   563	          meta: {
   564	            tool: 'memory_search',
   565	            truncated: true,
   566	            preserved: true,
   567	          },
   568	        },
   569	        {
   570	          summary: 'Context truncated to fit token budget',
   571	          data: {
   572	            count: minimalResults.length,
   573	            results: minimalResults,
   574	          },
   575	          meta: {
   576	            tool: 'memory_search',
   577	            truncated: true,
   578	            preserved: true,
   579	            metadataOnly: true,
   580	          },
   581	        },
   582	      ];
   583	    };
   584	
   585	    const emptyCandidates: Array<Record<string, unknown>> = [
   586	      {
   587	        summary: 'Context truncated to fit token budget',
   588	        data: {
   589	          count: 0,
   590	          results: [],
   591	        },
   592	        meta: {
   593	          tool: 'memory_search',
   594	          truncated: true,
   595	          parseFailed: Boolean(parseFailedInnerText),
   596	        },
   597	      },
   598	      {
   599	        data: {
   600	          count: 0,
   601	          results: [],
   602	        },
   603	        meta: {
   604	          tool: 'memory_search',
   605	          truncated: true,
   606	        },
   607	      },
   608	      {
   609	        data: {
   610	          count: 0,
   611	          results: [],
   612	        },
   613	      },
   614	    ];
   615	
   616	    const candidateInnerStates: Array<Record<string, unknown>> = [
   617	      ...buildPreservedCandidates(),
   618	      ...emptyCandidates,
   619	    ];
   620	
   621	    if (parseFailedInnerText) {
   622	      const meta = (emptyCandidates[0].meta as Record<string, unknown>);
   623	      meta.parseFailedPreview = parseFailedInnerText.slice(0, 120);
   624	    }
   625	
   626	    for (const innerEnvelope of candidateInnerStates) {
   627	      const candidateResults = (innerEnvelope.data as { results?: unknown[] } | undefined)?.results;
   628	      const candidateResultCount = Array.isArray(candidateResults) ? candidateResults.length : undefined;
   629	
   630	      if (contentClone.length > 0) {
   631	        contentClone[0] = { ...contentClone[0], text: JSON.stringify(innerEnvelope) };
   632	        (fallbackResult as Record<string, unknown>).content = contentClone;
   633	      } else {
   634	        (fallbackResult as Record<string, unknown>).content = [
   635	          { type: 'text', text: JSON.stringify(innerEnvelope) },
   636	        ];
   637	      }
   638	
   639	      if (estimateTokens(JSON.stringify(fallbackResult)) <= budgetTokens) {
   640	        if (candidateResultCount === 0) {
   641	          droppedAllResultsReason = 'impossible_budget';
   642	        }
   643	        return fallbackResult;
   644	      }
   645	    }
   646	
   647	    droppedAllResultsReason = 'impossible_budget';
   648	    return {
   649	      strategy: baseResult.strategy,
   650	      mode: baseResult.mode,
   651	      content: [{
   652	        type: 'text',
   653	        text: JSON.stringify({ data: { count: 0, results: [] } }),
   654	      }],
   655	    };
   656	  };
   657	
   658	  const compactStructuredResult = (
   659	    innerEnvelope: Record<string, unknown>,
   660	    currentResults: Array<Record<string, unknown>>,
   661	    contentEntries: Array<{ type: string; text: string }>,
   662	  ): { result: ContextResult; actualTokens: number } | null => {
   663	    const truncateKeys = ['content', 'snippet', 'summary', 'text'] as const;
   664	    const lastIndex = currentResults.length - 1;
   665	
   666	    if (lastIndex < 0) {
   667	      return null;
   668	    }
   669	
   670	    const lastResult = currentResults[lastIndex];
   671	    if (!lastResult || typeof lastResult !== 'object') {
   672	      return null;
   673	    }
   674	
   675	    for (const key of truncateKeys) {
   676	      const originalValue = lastResult[key];
   677	      if (typeof originalValue !== 'string' || originalValue.length === 0) {
   678	        continue;
   679	      }
   680	
   681	      let bestResult: ContextResult | null = null;
   682	      let bestTokens = Number.POSITIVE_INFINITY;
   683	      let low = 0;
   684	      let high = originalValue.length;
   685	
   686	      while (low <= high) {
   687	        const mid = Math.floor((low + high) / 2);
   688	        const candidateResults = [...currentResults];
   689	        candidateResults[lastIndex] = {
   690	          ...lastResult,
   691	          [key]: originalValue.slice(0, mid),
   692	        };
   693	
   694	        innerEnvelope.data = {
   695	          ...((innerEnvelope.data as Record<string, unknown>) ?? {}),
   696	          results: candidateResults,
   697	          count: candidateResults.length,
   698	        };
   699	
   700	        const candidateContent = contentEntries.map((entry, index) => (
   701	          index === 0 ? { type: entry.type, text: JSON.stringify(innerEnvelope) } : { ...entry }
   702	        ));
   703	        const candidateResult = {
   704	          ...truncatedResult,
   705	          content: candidateContent,
   706	        } as ContextResult;
   707	        const candidateTokens = estimateTokens(JSON.stringify(candidateResult));
   708	
   709	        if (candidateTokens <= budgetTokens) {
   710	          bestResult = candidateResult;
   711	          bestTokens = candidateTokens;
   712	          low = mid + 1;
   713	        } else {
   714	          high = mid - 1;
   715	        }
   716	      }
   717	
   718	      if (bestResult) {
   719	        return {
   720	          result: bestResult,
   721	          actualTokens: bestTokens,
   722	        };
   723	      }
   724	    }
   725	
   726	    return null;
   727	  };
   728	
   729	  // Try to find and truncate the inner results array
   730	  const contentArr = (truncatedResult as Record<string, unknown>).content as Array<{ type: string; text: string }> | undefined;
   731	  let parseFailedInnerText: string | undefined;
   732	  // REQ-002 (Cluster 1): Track survivors so the fallback path can preserve them
   733	  // instead of zero-filling.
   734	  let preservedAfterStructural: Array<Record<string, unknown>> = [];
   735	  if (contentArr && Array.isArray(contentArr) && contentArr.length > 0 && contentArr[0]?.text) {
   736	    try {
   737	      const innerEnvelope = JSON.parse(contentArr[0].text);
   738	      const innerResults = innerEnvelope?.data?.results;
   739	
   740	      if (Array.isArray(innerResults) && innerResults.length > 0) {
   741	        originalResultCount = innerResults.length;
   742	
   743	        // Results should already be sorted by score (highest first)
   744	        // Remove items from the end until we fit within budget
   745	        const currentResults = [...innerResults];
   746	        let currentTokens = preEnforcementTokens;
   747	
   748	        // Phase 1: Adaptive content truncation — truncate content fields before dropping results
   749	        const MAX_CONTENT_CHARS = 500;
   750	        for (const r of currentResults) {
   751	          if (r.content && typeof r.content === 'string' && r.content.length > MAX_CONTENT_CHARS) {
   752	            r.content = r.content.substring(0, MAX_CONTENT_CHARS) + '...';
   753	            r.contentTruncated = true;
   754	          }
   755	        }
   756	        // Re-estimate after content truncation
   757	        innerEnvelope.data.results = currentResults;
   758	        innerEnvelope.data.count = currentResults.length;
   759	        currentTokens = estimateTokens(JSON.stringify(innerEnvelope));
   760	
   761	        // Phase 2: Drop lowest-scored results if still over budget
   762	        while (currentResults.length > 1 && currentTokens > budgetTokens) {
   763	          // Remove the last (lowest-scored) result
   764	          const removed = currentResults.pop();
   765	          const removedTokens = estimateTokens(JSON.stringify(removed));
   766	          currentTokens -= removedTokens;
   767	        }
   768	
   769	        // Phase 3: Two-tier response — append metadata-only entries for dropped results
   770	        const droppedResults = innerResults.slice(currentResults.length);
   771	        if (droppedResults.length > 0) {
   772	          const metadataOnly = droppedResults.map((r: Record<string, unknown>) => ({
   773	            id: r.id,
   774	            title: r.title,
   775	            similarity: r.similarity,
   776	            specFolder: r.specFolder,
   777	            confidence: r.confidence,
   778	            importanceTier: r.importanceTier,
   779	            isConstitutional: r.isConstitutional,
   780	            metadataOnly: true,

   784	            currentResults.push(...metadataOnly);

   787	        }
   788

   821	        const compacted = compactStructuredResult(innerEnvelope, currentResults, contentArr);
   822	        if (compacted) {
   823	          return {
   824	            result: compacted.result,
   825	            enforcement: {
   826	              budgetTokens,
   827	              preEnforcementTokens,
   828	              returnedTokens: compacted.actualTokens,
   829	              actualTokens: compacted.actualTokens,
   830	              enforced: true,
   831	              truncated: true,
   832	              originalResultCount,
   833	              returnedResultCount,
   834	            }
   835	          };
   836	        }
   837	      }

   839	      parseFailed = true;

   841	      // JSON parse failed — fall through to structural truncation
   842	    }

   844	
   845	  // Fallback when parsing fails or a structured response still exceeds budget.
   846	  // Always emit valid nested JSON rather than raw character slices.

   848	  // truncation so it can keep them instead of silently zero-filling.
   849	  const fallbackResult = fallbackToStructuredBudget(
   850	    parseFailed ? result : truncatedResult,
   851	    parseFailedInnerText,
   852	    preservedAfterStructural,
   853	  );
   854	
   855	  const fallbackTokens = estimateTokens(JSON.stringify(fallbackResult));
   856	
   857	  // Re-extract the actual returned count from the fallback envelope so the
   858	  // metadata never advertises survivors that the payload no longer contains.
   859	  const extractedFallbackCount = extractNestedResultCount(fallbackResult);
   860	  const fallbackReturnedCount = extractedFallbackCount ?? returnedResultCount;
   861	  if (fallbackReturnedCount === 0 && !droppedAllResultsReason) {
   862	    droppedAllResultsReason = 'impossible_budget';
   863	  }
   864	
   865	  return {
   866	    result: fallbackResult,
   867	    enforcement: {
   868	      budgetTokens,
   869	      preEnforcementTokens,
   870	      returnedTokens: fallbackTokens,
   871	      actualTokens: fallbackTokens,
   872	      enforced: true,
   873	      truncated: true,
   874	      originalResultCount,
   875	      returnedResultCount: fallbackReturnedCount,
   876	      ...(droppedAllResultsReason ? { droppedAllResultsReason } : {}),
   877	    }
   878	  };

It estimates the serialized response, truncates oversized embedded `data.results`, compacts content fields, drops lowest-priority tail results, and falls back to minimal structured payloads if the budget is impossible.
